----- FILE: /opt/scalp/dp.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# ---------- CONFIG ----------
ROOT="/opt/scalp"
DUMP_DIR="${ROOT}/dump"
mkdir -p "$DUMP_DIR"
TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')"
OUT="${DUMP_DIR}/scalp_full_${TS}.txt"
MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB="${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB:-512}"

# ---------- GIT ENV ----------
[ -f /etc/scalp.env ] && . /etc/scalp.env
: "${GIT_USERNAME:?}"
: "${GIT_TOKEN:?}"
GIT_BRANCH="${GIT_BRANCH:-main}"
GIT_EMAIL_USE="${GIT_EMAIL:-${GIT_USERNAME}@users.noreply.github.com}"
REMOTE_URL="https://${GIT_HOST:-github.com}/${GIT_OWNER:-$GIT_USERNAME}/${GIT_REPO:-Scalp}.git"

# ---------- HEADER ----------
{
  echo "# ===== SCALP PROJECT DUMP ====="
  echo "# $(date -u +'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC')"
  echo "# Root: $ROOT"
  echo
  echo "========== TREE =========="
} > "$OUT"

find "$ROOT" -type f \
  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/venv/*' \
  -not -path '*/dump/*' -not -path '*/logs/*' \
  -size -"${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB}"k \
  \( -name '*.py' -o -name '*.sh' -o -name '*.conf' -o -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.txt' \) |
  sort | while IFS= read -r f; do
    sz=$(stat -c%s "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    mt=$(stat -c%y "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo unknown)
    printf "%-80s %12s %s\n" "$f" "$sz" "$mt" >> "$OUT"
done

{
  echo
  echo "========== FILE CONTENT =========="
} >> "$OUT"

find "$ROOT" -type f \
  -not -path '*/.git/*' -not -path '*/venv/*' \
  -not -path '*/dump/*' -not -path '*/logs/*' \
  -size -"${MAX_FILE_SIZE_KB}"k \
  \( -name '*.py' -o -name '*.sh' -o -name '*.conf' -o -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.txt' \) |
  sort | while IFS= read -r f; do
    echo -e "\n----- FILE: $f -----" >> "$OUT"
    cat "$f" 2>/dev/null >> "$OUT" || true
done

# ---------- DATABASE STRUCTURE (finale complète) ----------
{
  echo
  echo "========== DATABASE STRUCTURE =========="
} >> "$OUT"

for DB_PATH in /opt/scalp/project/data/*.db; do
  [ -s "$DB_PATH" ] || continue
  echo -e "\n----- DATABASE: $DB_PATH -----" >> "$OUT"

  {
    echo "-- TABLES --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" ".tables" 2>/dev/null || echo "(locked or unreadable)"
    echo

    for T in $(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" ".tables" 2>/dev/null); do
      echo "[TABLE: $T]"
      sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "PRAGMA table_info($T);" 2>/dev/null || true
      echo
    done

    echo "-- VIEWS --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='view' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no views)"
    echo

    echo "-- INDEXES --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='index' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no indexes)"
    echo

    echo "-- TRIGGERS --"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_PATH" "SELECT name, sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='trigger' ORDER BY name;" 2>/dev/null || echo "(no triggers)"
    echo
  } >> "$OUT"
done

# ---------- GIT PUSH ----------
cd "$ROOT"
git rev-parse --is-inside-work-tree >/dev/null 2>&1 || git init -q .
git config user.name "$GIT_USERNAME"
git config user.email "$GIT_EMAIL_USE"
git remote get-url origin >/dev/null 2>&1 || git remote add origin "$REMOTE_URL"

git add -f "$OUT"
git commit -m "dump ${TS}" || true
AUTH_URL="https://${GIT_USERNAME}:${GIT_TOKEN}@${REMOTE_URL#https://}"
git push -f "$AUTH_URL" HEAD:"$GIT_BRANCH"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/OB_collect.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_U="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_collect.log"

echo "[$(date)] OB_COLLECT START" >> "$LOG"

# load universe
mapfile -t UNIVERSE < <(sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_U" "SELECT instId FROM universe;")

# transform AAVE/USDT → AAVEUSDT_UMCBL
convert_inst() {
    echo "${1//\//}"_UMCBL
}

while true; do
    for inst in "${UNIVERSE[@]}"; do
        sym=$(convert_inst "$inst")

        URL="https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/candles?symbol=${sym}&granularity=60"
        JSON=$(curl -s "$URL")

        # Check valid response (must be array)
        if echo "$JSON" | jq -e '.[0]' >/dev/null 2>&1; then
            ts=$(echo "$JSON" | jq -r '.[0][0]')
            o=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][1]')
            h=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][2]')
            l=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][3]')
            c=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][4]')
            v=$(echo "$JSON"  | jq -r '.[0][5]')

            sqlite3 "$DB_OB" <<SQL
INSERT INTO ohlcv_1m(instId, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
VALUES("$sym", $ts, $o, $h, $l, $c, $v)
ON CONFLICT(instId, ts) DO UPDATE SET
    o=excluded.o,
    h=excluded.h,
    l=excluded.l,
    c=excluded.c,
    v=excluded.v;
SQL

        else
            echo "[$(date)] ERR $sym Invalid JSON: $JSON" >> "$LOG"
        fi
    done

    sleep 1
done

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

# Sécurité: vérifier que la base n'est pas verrouillée
if lsof "$DB" | grep -q ob.db; then
  echo "❌ ob.db en cours d'utilisation. Ferme les processus avant d'agréger."
  lsof "$DB"
  exit 1
fi

sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;

-- (Optionnel mais recommandé si non créés) Index pour accélérer l'agrégation
-- CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ohlcv_1m_inst_ts ON ohlcv_1m(instId, ts);

-- Nettoyage 3m
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;

-- Agrégation 1m -> 3m sans fonctions analytiques (compat SQLite 3.37)
WITH g AS (
  SELECT
    instId,
    (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts3,
    MIN(ts) AS ts_min,
    MAX(ts) AS ts_max,
    MAX(h) AS h,
    MIN(l) AS l,
    SUM(v) AS v
  FROM ohlcv_1m
  GROUP BY instId, ts3
)
INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m(instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
SELECT
  g.instId,
  g.ts3 AS ts,
  (SELECT o FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=g.instId AND ts=g.ts_min) AS o,
  g.h,
  g.l,
  (SELECT c FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=g.instId AND ts=g.ts_max) AS c,
  g.v
FROM g;

-- Vérification
SELECT '3m' AS tf, COUNT(*) AS rows, datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts
FROM ohlcv_3m;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
clear
echo "===== DASH B_SIGNALS ====="
echo

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 10 6 10 10 10 8 20
SELECT instId   AS COIN,
       side     AS SIDE,
       reason   AS REASON,
       price    AS PRICE,
       atr      AS ATR,
       ROUND(score_B,2) AS SCORE_B,
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS TS_LOCAL
FROM signals_B
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
LIMIT 20;
SQL

echo
echo "----- SUMMARY GLOBAL -----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers off
.mode column
SELECT
  'BUY :'  || COUNT(*)  FILTER (WHERE side='buy')  || '   ' ||
  'SELL :' || COUNT(*)  FILTER (WHERE side='sell') AS "SIGNALS"
FROM signals_B;

SELECT 'LAST SIGNAL :' || instId || ' ' || side || ' ' ||
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
FROM signals_B ORDER BY ts_signal DESC LIMIT 1;

SELECT 'AVG AGE (s): ' ||
       printf("%.1f",AVG((strftime('%s','now')*1000-ts_signal)/1000.0))
FROM signals_B;
SQL

echo
echo "----- SUMMARY BY COIN -----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 10 8 8 10
SELECT instId AS COIN,
       COUNT(*) AS N,
       ROUND(AVG(score_B),2) AS AVG_SCORE,
       datetime(MAX(ts_signal)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS LAST_TS
FROM signals_B
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY N DESC
LIMIT 15;
SQL

echo
echo "----- SUMMARY BY REASON -----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 12 8 8 10
SELECT reason AS REASON,
       COUNT(*) AS N,
       ROUND(AVG(score_B),2) AS AVG_SCORE,
       datetime(MAX(ts_signal)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS LAST_TS
FROM signals_B
GROUP BY reason
ORDER BY N DESC
LIMIT 15;
SQL

echo "-----------------------------"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_diag_full.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_U="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

echo "====================================================="
echo "           DIAGNOSTIC COMPLET — B ANALYSE"
echo "====================================================="

echo
echo "---- 1. FEAT FRAICHEUR / COMPLETUDE ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" "
SELECT 'feat_1m', COUNT(*), MAX(ts),
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM feat_1m;
SELECT 'feat_3m', COUNT(*), MAX(ts),
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM feat_3m;
SELECT 'feat_5m', COUNT(*), MAX(ts),
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM feat_5m;
"

echo
echo "---- 2. FEAT MANQUANTS SUR UNIVERS ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_U' AS U;
WITH uni AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM U.universe
),
f AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM feat_1m GROUP BY 1
)
SELECT u.inst
FROM uni u
LEFT JOIN f ON f.inst = u.inst
WHERE f.inst IS NULL
ORDER BY u.inst;
DETACH DATABASE U;
SQL

echo
echo "---- 3. JOINTURE CTX ↔ FEAT ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_A' AS A;
WITH feat AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM feat_1m GROUP BY 1
),
ctx AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM A.ctx_a_latest GROUP BY 1
)
SELECT 
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat) AS n_feat,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ctx)  AS n_ctx,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat JOIN ctx USING(inst)) AS matches,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat) - (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat JOIN ctx USING(inst)) AS feat_without_ctx,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ctx ) - (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat JOIN ctx USING(inst)) AS ctx_without_feat;
DETACH DATABASE A;
SQL

echo
echo "---- 4. AGE CTX ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_A" "
SELECT instId,
       MAX(ts) AS ts,
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM ctx_a_latest
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY age_s DESC
LIMIT 15;
"

echo
echo "---- 5. AGE DERNIERS SIGNALS ----"
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" "
SELECT instId,
       side,
       reason,
       score_B,
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_signal)/1000.0,1) AS age_s,
       datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
FROM signals_B
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC
LIMIT 20;
"

echo
echo "---- 6. TRIGGERS PAR COIN (check skip / invalid) ----"
python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_triggers.py --diag 2>/dev/null || echo "B_triggers.py ne supporte pas --diag"

echo
echo "====================================================="
echo "                 FIN DIAGNOSTIC"
echo "====================================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_gate_counter.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_B=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db
DB_A=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
DB_U=/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db

echo "===== B GATE COUNTER ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="
sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_A' AS A;
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_U' AS U;

.headers on
.mode column

-- Gate#1: candidats (universe ∩ feat_1m frais)
WITH uni AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId FROM U.universe
),
feat_latest AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_feat
  FROM feat_1m GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
g1 AS (
  SELECT u.instId, f.ts_feat
  FROM uni u JOIN feat_latest f ON f.instId=u.instId
  WHERE (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - f.ts_feat) <= 120000
),
-- Gate#2: ctx frais
ctx_latest AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_ctx
  FROM A.ctx_a_latest GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
g2 AS (
  SELECT g1.instId, g1.ts_feat, c.ts_ctx
  FROM g1 LEFT JOIN ctx_latest c ON c.instId=g1.instId
  WHERE (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - c.ts_ctx) <= 300000
),
-- Gate#3: signal produit <= 600s
sig_latest AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, MAX(ts_signal) AS ts_sig
  FROM signals_B GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
)
SELECT
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM U.universe)                      AS universe,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM g1)                              AS g1_feat_ok,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM g2)                              AS g2_ctx_ok,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM g2 JOIN sig_latest s USING(instId)
     WHERE (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - s.ts_sig) <= 600000) AS g3_sig_ok;

DETACH DATABASE A;
DETACH DATABASE U;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_join_verify.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
echo "=== VERIFY A(ctx) ↔ B(feat) normalized join ==="
sqlite3 /opt/scalp/project/data/b.db <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db' AS A;
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT 
  (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT REPLACE(instId,'/','')) FROM feat_1m) AS feat_coins,
  (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT REPLACE(instId,'/','')) FROM A.ctx_a_latest) AS ctx_coins,
  (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (
      SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM feat_1m GROUP BY 1
  ) f
  JOIN (
      SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst FROM A.ctx_a_latest GROUP BY 1
  ) c USING(inst)) AS join_matches_norm;
DETACH DATABASE A;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_mini_dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

echo "====================================================="
echo "                 MINI-DASH B (10 min)"
echo "====================================================="

# --------------------------------------------------------
# 1. TOP 4 meilleurs score B
# --------------------------------------------------------
echo
echo "---- TOP 4 SCORE_B (ALL COINS) ----"

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId,
       side,
       reason,
       score AS score_B,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
FROM triggers
WHERE ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 600000
ORDER BY score DESC
LIMIT 4;
SQL

# --------------------------------------------------------
# 2. NOMBRE PAR TRIGGER (10 minutes)
# --------------------------------------------------------
echo
echo "---- COUNT BY TRIGGER (LAST 10 min) ----"

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT reason,
       COUNT(*) AS n
FROM triggers
WHERE ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 600000
GROUP BY reason
ORDER BY n DESC;
SQL

# --------------------------------------------------------
# 3. NOMBRE PAR COIN (10 minutes)
# --------------------------------------------------------
echo
echo "---- COUNT BY COIN (LAST 10 min) ----"

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId,
       COUNT(*) AS n
FROM triggers
WHERE ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 600000
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY n DESC
LIMIT 20;
SQL

# --------------------------------------------------------
# 4. TOTALS
# --------------------------------------------------------
echo
echo "---- TOTALS ----"

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM triggers
        WHERE ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 600000) AS total_10min,
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM triggers) AS total_all;
SQL

echo
echo "====================================================="
echo "                     END DASH"
echo "====================================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_sources_probe.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_B=/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db
DB_A=/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db
DB_OA=/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db
DB_U=/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db

echo "===== B SOURCES PROBE ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_A'  AS A;
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_OA' AS OA;
ATTACH DATABASE '$DB_U'  AS U;

.headers on
.mode column
.width 11 8 8 8 19 10 19 10 19 10

WITH uni AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId FROM U.universe
),
feat AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_feat
  FROM feat_1m
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
ctx AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_ctx
  FROM A.ctx_a_latest
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
sig AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts_signal) AS ts_sig
  FROM signals_B
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
oa5 AS (
  SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId,
         MAX(ts) AS ts_oa5
  FROM OA.ohlcv_5m
  GROUP BY REPLACE(instId,'/','')
),
mix AS (
  SELECT u.instId,
         f.ts_feat,
         c.ts_ctx,
         o.ts_oa5,
         s.ts_sig
  FROM uni u
  LEFT JOIN feat f ON f.instId=u.instId
  LEFT JOIN ctx  c ON c.instId=u.instId
  LEFT JOIN oa5  o ON o.instId=u.instId
  LEFT JOIN sig  s ON s.instId=u.instId
)
SELECT
  instId AS COIN,
  printf('%9.1f', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_feat)/1000.0) AS age_feat_s,
  printf('%9.1f', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_ctx )/1000.0) AS age_ctx_s,
  printf('%9.1f', (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_oa5)/1000.0) AS age_oa5_s,
  datetime(ts_feat/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_feat,
  CASE WHEN (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_feat) <= 120000 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'OLD' END AS gate_feat,
  datetime(ts_ctx/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ctx,
  CASE WHEN (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_ctx ) <= 300000 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'OLD' END AS gate_ctx,
  datetime(ts_sig/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_sig,
  CASE WHEN (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts_sig ) <= 600000 THEN 'OK' ELSE 'OLD' END AS gate_sig
FROM mix
ORDER BY age_sig_s IS NULL, gate_feat DESC, gate_ctx DESC, age_feat_s DESC
LIMIT 25;

.print ''
.print '--- GATES SUMMARY (Universe only) ---'
.headers off
SELECT 'Universe coins: ' || COUNT(*) FROM U.universe;
SELECT 'feat_1m fresh <=120s: ' || COUNT(*) FROM (
  SELECT 1 FROM feat_1m f
  JOIN U.universe u ON REPLACE(f.instId,'/','')=REPLACE(u.instId,'/','')
  GROUP BY REPLACE(f.instId,'/','')
  HAVING (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(f.ts)) <= 120000
);
SELECT 'ctx_a_latest fresh <=300s: ' || COUNT(*) FROM (
  SELECT 1 FROM A.ctx_a_latest a
  JOIN U.universe u ON REPLACE(a.instId,'/','')=REPLACE(u.instId,'/','')
  GROUP BY REPLACE(a.instId,'/','')
  HAVING (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(a.ts)) <= 300000
);
SELECT 'signals_B updated <=600s: ' || COUNT(*) FROM (
  SELECT 1 FROM signals_B s
  JOIN U.universe u ON REPLACE(s.instId,'/','')=REPLACE(u.instId,'/','')
  GROUP BY REPLACE(s.instId,'/','')
  HAVING (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(s.ts_signal)) <= 600000
);

DETACH DATABASE A;
DETACH DATABASE OA;
DETACH DATABASE U;
SQL

echo
echo "Hint: si seuls 1-2 coins sont 'OK' en feat/ctx, c'est amont (OA/A). Si feat/ctx OK mais sig OLD, c'est B_signals."

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/b_triggers_diag.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_U="/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"

echo "====================================================="
echo "         DIAG B — POURQUOI 0 SIGNALS ?"
echo "====================================================="

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_U" "SELECT instId FROM universe;" | while read inst; do
    norm="${inst//\//}"

    echo
    echo "----- $inst -----"

    # 1. fetch feat 1m
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId,
       ts,
       macd, macdsignal, macdhist,
       rsi,
       ema9, ema21, ema50,
       bb_up, bb_mid, bb_low,
       atr
FROM feat_1m
WHERE instId='$inst'
ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1;
SQL

    # 2. fetch ctx
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_A" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT instId, ctx, ts
FROM ctx_a_latest
WHERE instId='$inst';
SQL

    # 3. run B_triggers single coin
    python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_triggers.py --one "$inst" 2>/dev/null || echo "B_triggers n'a pas l'option --one"

done

echo
echo "====================================================="
echo "            FIN DIAG B — détail coin"
echo "====================================================="

SELECT '1m', MAX(ts), strftime('%H:%M:%S', (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)), 'unixepoch') AS age_hms FROM feat_1m;

SELECT '5m', MAX(ts), strftime('%H:%M:%S', (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)), 'unixepoch') AS age_hms FROM feat_5m;
"

echo "---- [5] 3 Derniers FEAT par TF ----"

echo
echo "3m:"
sqlite3 -header -column "$B_DB" "SELECT * FROM feat_3m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 3;"

echo
echo "5m:"
sqlite3 -header -column "$B_DB" "SELECT * FROM feat_5m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 3;"

echo
echo "---- [6] Vérification SERVICE ----"
systemctl status scalp-b-feat.service --no-pager || true

echo
echo "==========================================="
echo "           FIN CHECK B FEAT"
echo "==========================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/dash.log"
now_s=$(date +%s)
ts_now="$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
printf "\n===== SCALP PIPE HEALTH %s =====\n" "$(date '+%H:%M:%S')" | tee -a "$LOG"

check_db() {
    local name="$1" file="$2" table="$3" ts_col="$4"
    if [[ ! -f "$file" ]]; then
        printf "%-10s ❌ no DB found\n" "$name" | tee -a "$LOG"
        return
    fi
    local count ts_last age_s h m s age_hms status
    count=$(sqlite3 "$file" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    ts_last=$(sqlite3 "$file" "SELECT MAX($ts_col)/1000 FROM $table;")
    [[ -z "$ts_last" || "$ts_last" == "0" ]] && ts_last=$now_s
    age_s=$(( now_s - ${ts_last%.*:-0} ))
    h=$((age_s/3600)); m=$(( (age_s%3600)/60 )); s=$((age_s%60))
    age_hms=$(printf "%02dh%02dm%02ds" "$h" "$m" "$s")

    if (( age_s < 10 )); then status="✅"
    elif (( age_s < 60 )); then status="⚠️"
    else status="❌"
    fi

    printf "%-10s %s  %4s recs | last=%s | age=%s\n" \
        "$name" "$status" "$count" "$(date '+%H:%M:%S' -d @$ts_last 2>/dev/null || date -r "$ts_last" '+%H:%M:%S')" "$age_hms" \
        | tee -a "$LOG"
}

check_db "opener"   "$DATA/opener.db"   "trades_open_init" "ts_create"
check_db "follower" "$DATA/follower.db" "trades_follow"    "ts_update"
check_db "closer"   "$DATA/closer.db"   "trades_close"     "ts_close"
check_db "recorder" "$DATA/recorder.db" "trades_record"    "ts_record"

printf "==============================================\n" | tee -a "$LOG"
echo "" >> "$LOG"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash_b_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
NOW_MS=$(($(date +%s) * 1000))

hr() { printf "%s\n" "-------------------------------------------"; }

# ------------------------------
# 1. OB stats
# ------------------------------
ob_rows_1m=$(sqlite3 $DB_OB "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_1m;")
ob_rows_3m=$(sqlite3 $DB_OB "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_3m;")
ob_rows_5m=$(sqlite3 $DB_OB "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ohlcv_5m;")

ob_last_1m=$(sqlite3 $DB_OB "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_1m;")
ob_last_3m=$(sqlite3 $DB_OB "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_3m;")
ob_last_5m=$(sqlite3 $DB_OB "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_5m;")

age() {
    local last=$1
    echo $(( (NOW_MS - last) / 1000 ))
}

# ------------------------------
# 2. FEAT stats
# ------------------------------
feat_rows_1m=$(sqlite3 $DB_B "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat_1m;")
feat_rows_3m=$(sqlite3 $DB_B "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat_3m;")
feat_rows_5m=$(sqlite3 $DB_B "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM feat_5m;")

feat_last_1m=$(sqlite3 $DB_B "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_1m;")
feat_last_3m=$(sqlite3 $DB_B "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_3m;")
feat_last_5m=$(sqlite3 $DB_B "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_5m;")

# ------------------------------
# PRINT
# ------------------------------
echo "==========================================="
echo "      MINI DASH — B FEAT (1m/3m/5m)"
echo "==========================================="

echo
echo "---- [OB OHLCV] ----"
printf "1m | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$ob_rows_1m" "$(age $ob_last_1m)"
printf "3m | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$ob_rows_3m" "$(age $ob_last_3m)"
printf "5m | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$ob_rows_5m" "$(age $ob_last_5m)"

echo
echo "---- [FEAT] ----"
printf "1m | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$feat_rows_1m" "$(age $feat_last_1m)"
printf "3m | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$feat_rows_3m" "$(age $feat_last_3m)"
printf "5m | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$feat_rows_5m" "$(age $feat_last_5m)"

echo
echo "---- [STATUS] ----"
a1=$(age $feat_last_1m)
a3=$(age $feat_last_3m)
a5=$(age $feat_last_5m)

status="OK"
[ "$a1" -gt 300 ] && status="⚠️ 1m lag"
[ "$a3" -gt 900 ] && status="⚠️ 3m lag"
[ "$a5" -gt 900 ] && status="⚠️ 5m lag"

echo "$status"

echo
echo "==========================================="
echo "              FIN MINI DASH"
echo "==========================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash_ob_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

age() {
  ts_ms="$1"
  now_ms=$(($(date +%s) * 1000))
  echo $(( (now_ms - ts_ms) / 1000 ))
}

echo "==========================================="
echo "      MINI DASH — OB + FEAT (1m/3m/5m)"
echo "==========================================="

### OB OHLCV ###
echo "---- [OB OHLCV] ----"

for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    table="ohlcv_${tf}"
    rows=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    last_ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM $table;")
    if [[ -z "$last_ts" || "$last_ts" == "0" ]]; then age_s="n/a"
    else age_s=$(age "$last_ts")
    fi
    printf "%-3s | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$tf" "$rows" "$age_s"
done

### FEAT ###
echo "---- [FEAT] ----"

for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    table="feat_${tf}"
    rows=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $table;")
    last_ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM $table;")
    if [[ -z "$last_ts" || "$last_ts" == "0" ]]; then age_s="n/a"
    else age_s=$(age "$last_ts")
    fi
    printf "%-3s | rows=%-6s age=%4ss\n" "$tf" "$rows" "$age_s"
done


### STATUS ###
echo "---- [STATUS] ----"

ok=true
msg=""

# seuils
S1=120   # 1m max age
S3=180   # 3m max age
S5=300   # 5m max age  (corrigé)

check_tf() {
  tf="$1"; ob="$2"; ft="$3"; max="$4"
  if (( ob > max )); then ok=false; msg="$msg ⚠️ OB ${tf} lag (${ob} s)\n"; fi
  if (( ft > max )); then ok=false; msg="$msg ⚠️ FEAT ${tf} lag (${ft} s)\n"; fi
}

# ages
ob1=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_1m;")")
ft1=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM feat_1m;")")

ob3=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_3m;")")
ft3=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM feat_3m;")")

ob5=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM ohlcv_5m;")")
ft5=$(age "$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT IFNULL(MAX(ts),0) FROM feat_5m;")")

check_tf 1m "$ob1" "$ft1" "$S1"
check_tf 3m "$ob3" "$ft3" "$S3"
check_tf 5m "$ob5" "$ft5" "$S5"

if $ok; then
    echo "🟢 OK"
else
    echo -e "$msg"
fi


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/dash_ob_feat_coin.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

COIN="${1:-BTC/USDT}"

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

echo "====================================================="
echo "        DASH OB + FEAT — $COIN (1m / 3m / 5m)"
echo "====================================================="

for TF in 1m 3m 5m; do
    echo
    echo "-------------------- OHLCV $TF ----------------------"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_OB" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT ts,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS local,
       o,h,l,c,v
FROM ohlcv_${TF}
WHERE instId='${COIN}'
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

    echo
    echo "-------------------- FEAT $TF ------------------------"
    sqlite3 -readonly "$DB_B" <<SQL
.headers on
.mode column
SELECT ts,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS local,
       c,
       ema12, ema26,
       macd, macdsignal, macdhist,
       rsi14_1m AS rsi,
       atr14  AS atr,
       bb_mid, bb_up, bb_low, bb_width,
       mom, roc, slope_ema12_1m AS slope,
       ctx
FROM feat_${TF}
WHERE instId='${COIN}'
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

done

echo "====================================================="
echo "                       END"
echo "====================================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/diag_step_by_step.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/diag_step.log"
DATA="/opt/scalp/project/data"
SCRIPTS="/opt/scalp/project/scripts"
BIN="/opt/scalp/project/bin"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")"

stamp(){ printf "[%s] %s\n" "$(date '+%F %T')" "$*" | tee -a "$LOG"; }
run(){   printf "\n$ %s\n" "$*"       | tee -a "$LOG"; eval "$*"           | tee -a "$LOG"; }

stamp "=== STEP 0: ENV ==="
run "python3 -V"
run "sqlite3 -version"
run "ls -lh $DATA"
run "ls -lh $SCRIPTS"

stamp "=== STEP 1: SCHEMA REFRESH ==="
if [[ -x "$SCRIPTS/gen_schema_ref.sh" ]]; then
  run "bash $SCRIPTS/gen_schema_ref.sh"
else
  stamp "gen_schema_ref.sh absent → SKIP"
fi
test -s "$DATA/schema_ref.sql" || { stamp "schema_ref.sql manquant"; exit 1; }

stamp "=== STEP 2: SCHEMA CHECK (colonnes) ==="
if [[ -x "$SCRIPTS/diag_schema.py" ]]; then
  run "python3 $SCRIPTS/diag_schema.py"
elif [[ -x "$SCRIPTS/check_schema_all.py" ]]; then
  run "python3 $SCRIPTS/check_schema_all.py"
else
  stamp "diag_schema.py / check_schema_all.py absents → SKIP"
fi

stamp "=== STEP 3: INTEGRITY CHECK SQLite ==="
for db in "$DATA"/*.db; do
  [[ -s "$db" ]] || continue
  stamp "PRAGMA integrity_check → $(basename "$db")"
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$db\" \"PRAGMA integrity_check;\""
done

stamp "=== STEP 4: COMPILATION PYTHON ==="
find "$SCRIPTS" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name "*.py" | sort | while read -r f; do
  stamp "py_compile: $(basename "$f")"
  run "python3 -m py_compile \"$f\""
done

stamp "=== STEP 5: PIPELINE QUICK VIEWS (colonnes 100% existantes) ==="
# [O] trades_open_init (schéma_ref: instId, side, entry, sl, tp, ts_open, status, reason, score, confidence, ctx, ts_create)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/opener.db" ".tables" | grep -qw trades_open_init; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/opener.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,entry,sl,tp,status,datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open FROM trades_open_init ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

# [F] follow_snapshot (schéma_ref: trade_uid,instId,side,entry,price,pnl_float,sl,tp,ts_update,reason_close,trigger_BE,trigger_SLtrail,trigger_PYRAMID,trigger_TIMEOUT)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/follower.db" \".tables\" | grep -qw follow_snapshot; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/follower.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,entry,price,pnl_float,sl,tp,datetime(ts_update/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_update FROM follow_snapshot ORDER BY ts_update DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

# [C] trades_closed (schéma_ref: id,instId,side,pnl_real,ts_close,ts_open_ref)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/closer.db" ".tables" | grep -qw trades_closed; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/closer.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,pnl_real,datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_close FROM trades_closed ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

# [R] trades_recorded (schéma_ref: trade_uid,instId,side,entry,exit,pnl_real,reason_exit,ts_open,ts_close,ctx,score_B,score_A,score_U,recorded_at)
if sqlite3 -readonly "$DATA/recorder.db" ".tables" | grep -qw trades_recorded; then
  run "sqlite3 -readonly \"$DATA/recorder.db\" -header -column \"SELECT instId,side,entry,exit,pnl_real,reason_exit,datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_close FROM trades_recorded ORDER BY ts_close DESC LIMIT 5;\""
fi

stamp "=== STEP 6: SCRIPTS BIN ==="
[[ -x "$BIN/check_pipeline_full.sh"     ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_pipeline_full.sh"     || stamp "check_pipeline_full.sh SKIP"
[[ -x "$BIN/check_pipeline_timing.sh"   ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_pipeline_timing.sh"   || stamp "check_pipeline_timing.sh SKIP"
[[ -x "$BIN/check_post_opener.sh"       ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_post_opener.sh"       || stamp "check_post_opener.sh SKIP"
[[ -x "$BIN/check_signals_integrity.sh" ]] && run "bash $BIN/check_signals_integrity.sh" || stamp "check_signals_integrity.sh SKIP"

stamp "=== STEP 7: SELF-TESTS (--self-test si dispo) ==="
for f in "$SCRIPTS"/*.py; do
  grep -q -- "--self-test" "$f" || continue
  stamp "SELF-TEST: $(basename "$f")"
  run "python3 \"$f\" --self-test"
done

stamp "=== DONE ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/diagnostic_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

echo "==========================================="
echo "       SCALP — CHECK B FEAT (1m/3m/5m)"
echo "==========================================="

echo
echo "---- [1] Vérification OB OHLCV ----"
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    tbl="ohlcv_${tf}"
    cnt=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $tbl;")
    echo "$tf|$cnt"
done

echo
echo "---- [2] Fraîcheur OB ----"
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_${tf};")
    age=$(( ($(date +%s) - ts/1000) ))
    printf "%s|%s|%02d:%02d:%02d\n" "$tf" "$ts" "$((age/3600))" "$((age%3600/60))" "$((age%60))"
done

echo
echo "---- [3] Contenu FEAT ----"
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    tbl="feat_${tf}"
    cnt=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $tbl;")
    echo "$tbl|$cnt"
done

echo
echo "---- [4] Fraîcheur FEAT ----"
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_${tf};")
    age=$(( ($(date +%s) - ts/1000) ))
    printf "%s|%s|%02d:%02d:%02d\n" "$tf" "$ts" "$((age/3600))" "$((age%3600/60))" "$((age%60))"
done

echo
echo "---- [5] Vérification SERVICE ----"
systemctl status scalp-b-feat.service --no-pager || true

echo "==========================================="
echo "           FIN CHECK B FEAT"
echo "==========================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/maint_ohlcv.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/maint_ohlcv.log"
echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] START maintenance" >>"$LOG"

# --- Nettoyage (max rows) ---
sqlite3 "$DB" <<'SQL'
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_1m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 450
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_3m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
);
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m WHERE ts NOT IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_5m ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
);
VACUUM;
SQL

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] CLEAN OK" >>"$LOG"

# --- Ré-agrégation 3m ---
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/agg_3m_from_1m.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || echo "agg_3m fail" >>"$LOG"

# --- Vérification fraîcheur ---
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ohlcv_freshness.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1

echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] DONE maintenance" >>"$LOG"

  echo "[OA_HEALTH] ❌ OHLCV_5m too old ($age_s s) → restarting OA"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_aggregate_3m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOCK="/var/lock/ob_agg3m.lock"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_agg3m.log"

exec /usr/bin/flock -n "$LOCK" bash -c "
  echo \"\$(date '+%F %T') [AGG3M] Start aggregation\" >> \$LOG
  sqlite3 \$DB '
    DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;
    INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m (instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
    SELECT instId,
           (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts_group,
           first_value(o) OVER w AS o,
           MAX(h) OVER w AS h,
           MIN(l) OVER w AS l,
           last_value(c) OVER w AS c,
           SUM(v) OVER w AS v
    FROM ohlcv_1m
    WINDOW w AS (PARTITION BY instId, (ts/180000) ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN 2 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW)
    GROUP BY instId, ts_group;
  '
  echo \"\$(date '+%F %T') [AGG3M] Done\" >> \$LOG
"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_freshness.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

# TF -> (table:limit_age)
declare -A TF_TABLES=(
    ["1m"]="ohlcv_1m:60"
    ["3m"]="ohlcv_3m:180"
    ["5m"]="ohlcv_5m:300"
)

now_ms=$(($(date +%s) * 1000))

echo "=== LAST OB CANDLES USED ==="
printf "%-3s %-19s %-7s %s\n" "tf" "last_ts" "age_s" "status"
echo "--  -------------------  -------  -------"

for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    entry="${TF_TABLES[$tf]}"
    table="${entry%%:*}"
    limit="${entry##*:}"

    last_ts=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT MAX(ts) FROM $table;")

    if [[ -z "$last_ts" || "$last_ts" == "NULL" ]]; then
        printf "%-3s %-19s %-7s %s\n" "$tf" "---" "---" "❌"
        continue
    fi

    age=$(( (now_ms - last_ts) / 1000 ))
    last_human=$(date -d "@$((last_ts / 1000))" +"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

    status="⚠️"
    if (( age < limit )); then
        status="✅"
    fi

    printf "%-3s %-19s %-7d %s\n" "$tf" "$last_human" "$age" "$status"
done


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_hard_unlock.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "===== OB HARD UNLOCK ====="

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

echo "[1] Stop services"
systemctl stop scalp-ob.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-oa.service || true

echo "[2] Kill leftover Python processes"
pkill -9 -f OB_collect.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f OA_ohlcv_A.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f ob.db 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[3] Vérifie encore des locks"
lsof "$DB" || echo "(aucun lock détecté)"

echo "[4] Suppression fichiers WAL / SHM (force unlock)"
rm -f /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db-wal
rm -f /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db-shm

echo "[5] Test accès SQLite"
sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT 'OK_UNLOCK';"

echo "[6] RESET OHLCV"
sqlite3 "$DB" <<SQL
DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;
DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m;
VACUUM;
SQL

echo "[7] Restart OA + OB"
systemctl start scalp-oa.service
systemctl start scalp-ob.service

echo "===== DONE. Vérification dans 8s ====="
sleep 8

bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ohlcv_freshness.sh

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/ob_kill_all.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "=== KILL OB COLLECTOR + BUILDERS ==="

echo "[1] Stop systemd..."
systemctl stop scalp-ob-ws.service 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[2] Remove lock..."
rm -f /var/lock/ob_ws.lock 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[3] Kill all python processes related to OB_ws + builder..."
pkill -9 -f OB_ws_collect_v2.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f OB_ws_collect.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f ob_ws_singleton.sh 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -9 -f B_feat_builder_all.py 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[4] Double-kill (in case of forks)..."
for i in {1..5}; do
    pkill -9 -f OB_ws_collect_v2.py 2>/dev/null || true
    pkill -9 -f B_feat_builder_all.py 2>/dev/null || true
    sleep 0.2
done

echo "[5] Check remaining PIDs..."
pgrep -fl "OB_ws_collect|feat_builder|ob_ws" || echo "[OK] Aucun processus résiduel"

echo "[6] Check FD on ob.db..."
lsof /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db || echo "[OK] Aucun handle FD ouvert"

echo "=== CLEAN DONE ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/pipeline_diagnostics.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_O="/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
DB_F="/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_C="/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

sqlite3 "$DB_C" <<'SQL'
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_O"' AS O;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_F"' AS F;
ATTACH DATABASE '"$DB_B"' AS B;
.headers on
.mode column

WITH sig AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts) AS ts_signal_s
  FROM B.signals_B
  GROUP BY instId
),
open AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts_open) AS ts_open
  FROM O.trades_open_init
  GROUP BY instId
),
closed AS (
  SELECT instId, side, entry, exit, pnl, reason_exit, atr, ts_open, ts_close
  FROM main.positions_closed
)
SELECT
  c.instId,
  c.side,
  c.reason_exit,
  printf('%.4f', c.pnl) AS pnl,
  (c.ts_close - c.ts_open) AS trade_ms,
  CASE WHEN s.ts_signal_s IS NULL THEN NULL
       ELSE (c.ts_open - s.ts_signal_s*1000)
  END AS open_latency_ms
FROM closed c
LEFT JOIN sig s   ON s.instId = c.instId
LEFT JOIN open o  ON o.instId = c.instId AND o.ts_open = c.ts_open
ORDER BY c.ts_close DESC
LIMIT 50;

DETACH DATABASE O;
DETACH DATABASE F;
DETACH DATABASE B;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/rebuild_ob.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"

echo "[REBUILD_OB] → wipe old DB"
rm -f "$DB" "$DB-shm" "$DB-wal"

echo "[REBUILD_OB] → create new DB"
sqlite3 "$DB" << 'SQL'
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_1m (
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    o REAL, h REAL, l REAL, c REAL, v REAL,
    PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_3m (
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    o REAL, h REAL, l REAL, c REAL, v REAL,
    PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_5m (
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts     INTEGER NOT NULL,
    o REAL, h REAL, l REAL, c REAL, v REAL,
    PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_1m_ts  ON ohlcv_1m(ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_3m_ts  ON ohlcv_3m(ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_5m_ts  ON ohlcv_5m(ts);
SQL

echo "[REBUILD_OB] → smoke test"
sqlite3 "$DB" "SELECT name FROM sqlite_master;"

echo "[REBUILD_OB] DONE"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/rebuild_signals_for_open.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A="/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

echo "[SYNC] Import fresh ctx into b.db as ctx_cache"
sqlite3 "$DB_B" <<SQL
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ctx_cache;
CREATE TABLE ctx_cache AS
SELECT REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS instId, ctx, ts
FROM '${DB_A}'.ctx_a_latest;
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ctx_cache_instId ON ctx_cache(instId);
SQL

echo "[REBUILD] signals_for_open using ctx_cache"
sqlite3 "$DB_B" <<'SQL'
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS signals_for_open;
CREATE VIEW signals_for_open AS
SELECT
    b.id,
    b.instId,
    b.side,
    b.reason,
    COALESCE(c.ctx, 'unknown') AS ctx,
    b.price,
    b.atr,
    b.score_U,
    b.score_A,
    b.score_B,
    b.ts_signal,
    datetime(b.ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
    'pending' AS status
FROM signals_B b
LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c
  ON REPLACE(b.instId,'/','') = c.instId
WHERE b.ts_signal IS NOT NULL
ORDER BY b.ts_signal DESC;
SQL

echo "[OK] signals_for_open rebuilt successfully with ctx_cache"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/relaunch_ohlcv_feat.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "===== RELANCE OHLCV + FEAT ($(date '+%F %T')) ====="

# --- stop services ---
echo "[1] Stop services"
systemctl stop scalp-ob.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-oa.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-b-feat-builder.service || true
systemctl stop scalp-b-feat-builder.timer || true

# --- kill python leftover ---
echo "[2] Kill runaway processes"
pkill -f OB_collect.py || true
pkill -f OA_ohlcv_A.py || true
pkill -f B_feat_builder || true

# --- cleanup OHLCV if old ---
DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
echo "[3] Check OHLCV timestamps"

AGE1=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_1m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)
AGE5=$(sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM ohlcv_5m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)

if (( AGE1 > 300 || AGE5 > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️ OHLCV trop vieux → reset tables"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_OB" "DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m;"
else
    echo "OK OHLCV pas trop vieux"
fi

# --- cleanup feat if old ---
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
echo "[4] Check FEAT timestamps"

F1=$(sqlite3 "$DB_B" "SELECT (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts/1000)) FROM feat_1m;" 2>/dev/null || echo 999999)

if (( F1 > 300 )); then
    echo "⚠️ Features trop vieux → reset feat tables"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_1m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_3m;"
    sqlite3 "$DB_B" "DELETE FROM feat_5m;"
fi

# --- restart pipeline ---
echo "[5] Restart OA"
systemctl start scalp-oa.service

echo "[6] Restart OB"
systemctl start scalp-ob.service

echo "[7] Restart feat builder (timer)"
systemctl start scalp-b-feat-builder.timer

echo "===== RELANCE OK ====="

echo "[8] Vérification dans 10 secondes…"
sleep 10

echo "--- OHLCV FRESHNESS ---"
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_ohlcv_freshness.sh | sed 's/^/    /'

echo "--- FEAT FRESHNESS ---"
bash /opt/scalp/project/bin/check_feat_freshness.sh | sed 's/^/    /'


----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/restart_clean.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
echo "=== 🔄 REDÉMARRAGE PROPRE PIPELINE SCALP ==="

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data"

# --- 1️⃣ Arrêt des services
echo "[1/5] Arrêt des services..."
for svc in opener follower closer recorder ticks; do
  systemctl stop scalp-${svc}.service 2>/dev/null || true
done

# --- 2️⃣ Nettoyage des tables trades (si elles existent)
echo "[2/5] Nettoyage tables trades..."
sqlite3 ${DB}/opener.db   "DELETE FROM trades_open_init;" 2>/dev/null || true
sqlite3 ${DB}/follower.db "DELETE FROM trades_follow;"    2>/dev/null || true
sqlite3 ${DB}/closer.db   "DELETE FROM trades_closed;"    2>/dev/null || true
sqlite3 ${DB}/closer.db   "DELETE FROM positions_closed;" 2>/dev/null || true
sqlite3 ${DB}/recorder.db "DELETE FROM trades_history;"   2>/dev/null || true
sqlite3 ${DB}/budget.db   "DELETE FROM ledger;"           2>/dev/null || true

# --- 3️⃣ Réinitialisation du budget
echo "[3/5] Réinitialisation du budget à 1000 USDT..."
sqlite3 ${DB}/budget.db "
UPDATE budget_state
SET balance=1000.0,
    margin=0.0,
    pnl_real=0.0,
    ts_update=strftime('%s','now');
VACUUM;
"

# --- 4️⃣ Redémarrage des services dans l'ordre logique
echo "[4/5] Redémarrage des services..."
systemctl start scalp-ticks.service
sleep 5
systemctl start scalp-opener.service
sleep 2
systemctl start scalp-follower.service
sleep 2
systemctl start scalp-closer.service
sleep 2
systemctl start scalp-recorder.service
sleep 2

# --- 5️⃣ Vérification finale
echo "[5/5] Vérification état du budget et services..."
sqlite3 -header -column ${DB}/budget.db "SELECT * FROM budget_state;"
echo ""
systemctl --no-pager --plain list-units | grep scalp- | grep running || echo "⚠️ Certains services ne tournent pas."

echo ""
echo "=== ✅ PIPELINE SCALP RELANCÉ — BUDGET = 1000 USDT ==="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/scalp_ps.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "==============================================="
echo " SCALP — DIAGNOSTIC GLOBAL (services, timers, ps)"
echo " $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
echo "==============================================="

echo
echo "---- SYSTEMD SERVICES (SCALP) ----"
systemctl list-units --type=service --all | grep -E "scalp|SCALP|ticks|OB|OA|opener|closer|follower|recorder" || echo "Aucun service scalp trouvé"

echo
echo "---- SYSTEMD TIMERS (SCALP) ----"
systemctl list-timers --all | grep -E "scalp|SCALP|ticks|OB|OA" || echo "Aucun timer scalp"

echo
echo "---- PROCESS PYTHON RUNNING ----"
ps -ef | grep python | grep -E "T_ticks|OB_|OA_|B_|A_|follower|closer|recorder" | grep -v grep || echo "Aucun process Python scalp actif"

echo
echo "---- LOCKFILES PRESENT ----"
ls -l /var/lock | grep ob | grep -v grep || echo "Aucun lock OB"

echo
echo "---- SQLITE WAL/SHM FILES ----"
find /opt/scalp/project/data -maxdepth 1 -type f \( -name "*.db-wal" -o -name "*.db-shm" \) -ls || echo "Aucun WAL actif"

echo
echo "---- VERIFIER SI DB VERROUILLEES ----"
for db in /opt/scalp/project/data/*.db; do
    echo -n "$(basename "$db"): "
    sqlite3 "$db" "PRAGMA quick_check;" 2>&1 | head -n 1
done

echo
echo "---- TICKS (fraîcheur rapide) ----"
sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/t.db "
SELECT instId,
       lastPr,
       datetime(ts_ms/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS tick_time,
       age_hms
FROM v_ticks_latest
ORDER BY ts_ms DESC
LIMIT 10;
" || echo "Impossible de lire ticks"

echo
echo "---- OHLCV (TF1/TF5/TF3 dernière maj) ----"
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
  echo "TF $tf :"
  sqlite3 -readonly /opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db "
  SELECT instId,
         datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_ts,
         (strftime('%s','now') - MAX(ts)/1000) AS age_s
  FROM ohlcv_${tf}
  GROUP BY instId
  ORDER BY age_s ASC
  LIMIT 5;"
done

echo
echo "==============================================="
echo "   FIN DU DIAGNOSTIC SCALP"
echo "==============================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/sync_and_collect_1m.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_collect_sync.log"

# Attente du top minute exact
sec=$(date +%S)
if [ "$sec" != "00" ]; then
  wait=$((60 - sec))
  echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] attente ${wait}s pour top-minute..." | tee -a "$LOG"
  sleep $wait
fi

# Lancement de la collecte 1m
echo "[$(date '+%F %T')] lancement OB_collect.py (1m)" | tee -a "$LOG"
/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3 /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OB_collect.py --tf 1m >>"$LOG" 2>&1

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/sync_ctx_a_to_b.sql -----
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db' AS A;

-- Mise à jour de feat_1m.ctx avec le contexte réel de A
UPDATE feat_1m
SET ctx = (
    SELECT ctx_a.ctx
    FROM A.ctx_a_latest AS ctx_a
    WHERE REPLACE(ctx_a.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(feat_1m.instId,'/','')
)
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM A.ctx_a_latest AS ctx_a
    WHERE REPLACE(ctx_a.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(feat_1m.instId,'/','')
);

DETACH DATABASE A;

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

echo "======================================="
echo "   SCALP TICKS — RESET COMPLET"
echo "======================================="

echo "[1] Stop service…"
systemctl stop scalp-ticks.service 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[2] Kill all T_ticks.py…"
pkill -f T_ticks.py 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f ticks.py 2>/dev/null || true

echo "[3] Clean WAL/SHM…"
/bin/rm -f /opt/scalp/project/data/t.db-wal
/bin/rm -f /opt/scalp/project/data/t.db-shm

echo "[4] Quick check DB ticks structure…"
sqlite3 /opt/scalp/project/data/t.db "PRAGMA table_info(ticks);" || true

echo "[5] Start service…"
systemctl start scalp-ticks.service
sleep 2

echo "[6] Check systemd status…"
systemctl status scalp-ticks.service --no-pager | sed -n '1,12p'

echo "[7] Last 30 lines log…"
/usr/bin/tail -n 30 /opt/scalp/project/logs/ticks_daemon.log || true

echo "[8] Check LIVE ticks freshness (max 10 newest ticks)…"
sqlite3 /opt/scalp/project/data/t.db "
SELECT instId,lastPr,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS tick_time,
       printf('%02d:%02d:%02d',
             ((strftime('%s','now') - ts/1000)/3600),
             (((strftime('%s','now') - ts/1000)%3600)/60),
             ((strftime('%s','now') - ts/1000)%60)) AS age_hms
FROM ticks
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;
"

echo "======================================="
echo "     FIN DIAGNOSTIC TICKS"
echo "======================================="

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/bin/x_dash.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB="/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"
SERVICES=(
  scalp-signal.service
  scalp-opener.service
  scalp-follower.service
  scalp-closer.service
  scalp-recorder.service
  scalp-budget.service
  scalp-gest-bus.service
)

clear
echo "===== SCALP SYSTEM HEALTH DASH ====="
echo "📅 $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
echo

# ---- 1. SYSTEMD STATUS ----
printf "%-22s %-8s %-10s\n" "SERVICE" "STATUS" "PID"
echo "---------------------------------------------"

for svc in "${SERVICES[@]}"; do
  if systemctl is-active --quiet "$svc"; then
    pid=$(systemctl show -p MainPID --value "$svc")
    printf "%-22s ✅ %-8s %-10s\n" "$svc" "active" "$pid"
  else
    printf "%-22s ❌ %-8s\n" "$svc" "inactive"
  fi
done

echo
echo "---- 2. BUS EVENTS ----"

sqlite3 -readonly "$DB" <<'SQL'
.headers on
.mode column
.width 10 8 8 22
SELECT src AS MODULE,
       COUNT(*) AS TOTAL,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-300)*1000) AS LAST5MIN,
       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS LAST_EVENT
FROM bus_events
GROUP BY src
ORDER BY src;
SQL

echo
echo "---- 3. LATEST 10 EVENTS ----"

.headers off
.mode column
.width 10 14 14 22
SELECT src, instId, event, datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
FROM bus_events
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 10;
SQL

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/follower_pnl_float.sql -----
-- ===========================================
-- Vue : v_pnl_float
-- But : afficher le PnL flottant (non réalisé)
--       pour chaque position active ou ouverte
-- ===========================================

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_pnl_float;

CREATE VIEW v_pnl_float AS
SELECT
    f.instId,
    f.side,
    f.entry,
    t.lastPr AS last,
    ROUND(
        CASE
            WHEN f.side='buy'  THEN (t.lastPr - f.entry) * f.qty * f.leverage
            WHEN f.side='sell' THEN (f.entry - t.lastPr) * f.qty * f.leverage
            ELSE 0
        END, 6
    ) AS pnl_float_usdt,
    ROUND(f.qty * f.entry * f.leverage, 6) AS notional_usdt,
    datetime(t.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_tick
FROM trades_follow f
LEFT JOIN main.v_ticks_latest t
  ON REPLACE(t.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(f.instId,'/','')
WHERE f.status IN ('active','open');

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/init_bus.sql -----
-- =========================================================
--   SCALP CENTRAL BUS  —  Communication inter-modules
-- =========================================================

PRAGMA journal_mode = WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous = NORMAL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    stage TEXT NOT NULL,          -- ex: "B→GEST", "GEST→OPEN", etc.
    source TEXT NOT NULL,         -- module émetteur
    dest TEXT NOT NULL,           -- module récepteur
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,         -- ex: BTC/USDT
    payload TEXT,                 -- JSON libre
    ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
    ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_dest_ack ON bus(dest, ack);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_stage ON bus(stage);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_inst ON bus(instId);

-- VUES DE DIAGNOSTIC
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_pending AS
SELECT stage, dest, COUNT(*) AS pending
FROM bus
WHERE ack=0
GROUP BY stage, dest;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_last_msg AS
SELECT stage, dest, instId,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
       payload
FROM bus
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 50;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_pipeline_health AS
SELECT dest,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ack=0) AS pending,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ack=1) AS processed,
       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_activity
FROM bus
GROUP BY dest;

CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_activity_last_5min AS
SELECT stage, dest,
       COUNT(*) AS recent_msgs
FROM bus
WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-300)*1000
GROUP BY stage, dest;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/q_follow_pnl_float.sql -----
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db' AS tdb;

WITH ticks AS (
  SELECT
    instId,
    lastPr AS last,
    datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_last
  FROM tdb.v_ticks_latest
)
SELECT
  f.instId,
  f.side,
  ROUND(f.entry, 4) AS entry,
  ROUND(t.last, 4) AS last,
  ROUND(
    CASE
      WHEN f.side='buy'  THEN (t.last - f.entry) / f.entry * 100
      WHEN f.side='sell' THEN (f.entry - t.last) / f.entry * 100
      ELSE 0 END, 2
  ) AS pnl_pct,
  ROUND(
    CASE
      WHEN f.side='buy'  THEN (t.last - f.entry) * f.qty * f.leverage
      WHEN f.side='sell' THEN (f.entry - t.last) * f.qty * f.leverage
      ELSE 0 END, 2
  ) AS pnl_usdt,
  ROUND(f.tp, 4) AS tp,
  ROUND(f.sl, 4) AS sl,
  f.status,
  datetime(f.ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS opened_at,
  t.ts_last AS last_tick
FROM trades_follow f
LEFT JOIN ticks t
  ON REPLACE(f.instId,'/','') = REPLACE(t.instId,'/','')
WHERE f.status IN ('active','open','pending')
ORDER BY f.ts_open DESC;

DETACH DATABASE tdb;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/data/v_signals_coin_overview.sql -----
CREATE VIEW v_signals_coin_overview AS
WITH last_sig AS (
    SELECT 
        REPLACE(instId,'/','') AS inst_key,
        instId,
        side,
        reason AS trigger,
        score_B,
        ts_signal,
        datetime(ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
        printf('%02d:%02d:%02d',
               (strftime('%s','now') - ts_signal/1000)/3600,
               ((strftime('%s','now') - ts_signal/1000)/60)%60,
               (strftime('%s','now') - ts_signal/1000)%60) AS age_hms,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY REPLACE(instId,'/','') ORDER BY ts_signal DESC) AS rn
    FROM signals_B
)
SELECT 
    u.instId,
    COALESCE(c.ctx, 'unknown') AS ctx,
    ls.side,
    ls.trigger,
    ROUND(ls.score_B,2) AS score_B,
    ls.ts_local,
    ls.age_hms
FROM universe u
LEFT JOIN last_sig ls
  ON REPLACE(u.instId,'/','') = ls.inst_key AND ls.rn = 1
LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c
  ON REPLACE(u.instId,'/','') = c.instId
ORDER BY ls.ts_signal DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_analyse.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, math, time

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_U = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
TF = "5m"

def softmax(x):
    e = [math.exp(i) for i in x]
    s = sum(e)
    return [v/s for v in e]

def get_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_U)
    rows = con.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe ORDER BY instId").fetchall()
    con.close()
    return [r[0] for r in rows]

def load_ob(inst):
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    row = con.execute(f"SELECT rsi FROM ob_{TF} WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1", (inst,)).fetchone()
    con.close()
    return row[0] if row else None

def compute_ctx(rsi):
    if rsi < 30: return "bullish"
    if rsi > 70: return "bearish"
    if 45 <= rsi <= 55: return "range"
    return "none"

def compute_score_A(ctx):
    if ctx == "bullish": return 0.8
    if ctx == "bearish": return -0.8
    if ctx == "range": return 0.0
    return 0.0

def run():
    insts = get_universe()
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    out = []

    for inst in insts:
        rsi = load_ob(inst)
        if rsi is None:
            continue
        ctx = compute_ctx(rsi)
        score_A = compute_score_A(ctx)
        p_buy, p_sell = softmax([score_A, -score_A])
        out.append((inst, now, 0.0, score_A, p_buy, p_sell, ctx))

    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    con.execute("DELETE FROM ctx_a_latest")
    con.executemany("INSERT INTO ctx_a_latest(instId,ts,score_U,score_A,p_buy,p_sell,ctx) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)", out)
    con.commit()
    con.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run()

#!/usr/bin/env python3

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_ctx.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# SCALP - A CTX (contexte directionnel + intensité)
# score_U : ratio volume/volatilité (0→1)
# score_A : force du contexte directionnel (0→1)

import sqlite3
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import logging
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# ---------------------------------------
# LOGGING
# ---------------------------------------
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s A_CTX %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
        logging.FileHandler("/opt/scalp/project/logs/a_ctx.log", mode='a')
    ]
)

# ---------------------------------------
# DB CONNECT
# ---------------------------------------
def connect_db(path):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

# ---------------------------------------
# LOAD FEAT TABLES
# ---------------------------------------
def load_feat(conn, table):
    q = f"""
        SELECT instId, ts, ema12, ema26, macd, rsi14
        FROM {table}
        ORDER BY instId, ts;
    """
    return pd.read_sql_query(q, conn)

def load_ohlcv_with_volume(conn, table):
    q = f"""
        SELECT instId, ts, close, volume
        FROM {table}
        ORDER BY instId, ts;
    """
    return pd.read_sql_query(q, conn)

# ---------------------------------------
# COMPUTE SCORE_U : volume / volatilité
# ---------------------------------------
def compute_score_U(df_feat, df_ohlcv):
    df = df_feat.merge(df_ohlcv, on=["instId","ts"], how="inner")

    # volatilité : |close - ema26|
    df["volatility"] = (df["close"] - df["ema26"]).abs()

    df["raw_U"] = df["volume"] / (df["volatility"] + 1e-9)

    # NORMALISATION DOUCE
    df["score_U"] = np.tanh(df["raw_U"])

    return df[["instId","ts","score_U"]]

# ---------------------------------------
# SCORE TF DIRECTIONNEL
# ---------------------------------------
def compute_score_tf(df):
    # signaux directionnels simples
    s_ema  = np.tanh((df["ema12"] - df["ema26"]) / (1e-8 + abs(df["ema26"])))
    s_macd = np.tanh(df["macd"])
    s_rsi  = np.tanh((df["rsi14"] - 50) / 50)

    S = 0.5 * s_ema + 0.3 * s_macd + 0.2 * s_rsi
    return float(S)

# ---------------------------------------
# SOFTMAX DIRECTIONNEL
# ---------------------------------------
def softmax_ctx(S):
    e_buy  = np.exp(S)
    e_sell = np.exp(-S)
    e_rng  = 1.0

    Z = e_buy + e_sell + e_rng
    p_buy  = float(e_buy  / Z)
    p_sell = float(e_sell / Z)

    if p_buy >= max(p_sell, 1 - p_buy - p_sell):
        ctx = "bullish"
    elif p_sell >= max(p_buy, 1 - p_buy - p_sell):
        ctx = "bearish"
    else:
        ctx = "range"

    return p_buy, p_sell, ctx

# ---------------------------------------
# MAIN CTX PIPELINE
# ---------------------------------------
def main():
    logging.info("Start A_CTX (light)")

    conn_a  = connect_db("/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")
    conn_oa = connect_db("/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db")

    # Load features
    f5  = load_feat(conn_a, "feat_5m")
    f15 = load_feat(conn_a, "feat_15m")
    f30 = load_feat(conn_a, "feat_30m")

    # Load ohlcv for score_U
    ohlcv5 = load_ohlcv_with_volume(conn_oa, "ohlcv_5m")

    # Compute score_U
    dfU = compute_score_U(f5, ohlcv5)  # basé sur TF rapide (5m)
    dfU = dfU.groupby("instId").tail(1).set_index("instId")

    # Latest rows per TF
    f5_latest  = f5.groupby("instId").tail(1).set_index("instId")
    f15_latest = f15.groupby("instId").tail(1).set_index("instId")
    f30_latest = f30.groupby("instId").tail(1).set_index("instId")

    # Clear ctx table
    conn_a.execute("DELETE FROM ctx_a_latest;")

    ts_now = int(datetime.now().timestamp() * 1000)

    insts = sorted(f5_latest.index.unique())
    for inst in insts:
        try:
            r5  = f5_latest.loc[inst]
            r15 = f15_latest.loc[inst]
            r30 = f30_latest.loc[inst]
            u   = dfU.loc[inst]["score_U"]

            # Direction TF
            S5  = compute_score_tf(r5)
            S15 = compute_score_tf(r15)
            S30 = compute_score_tf(r30)

            # Fusion multi-TF
            S = 0.5*S5 + 0.3*S15 + 0.2*S30

            # score_A = force directionnelle (0→1)
            score_A = abs(S)

            # softmax
            p_buy, p_sell, ctx = softmax_ctx(S)

            logging.info(f"{inst} S={S:.4f} scoreU={u:.3f} pbuy={p_buy:.3f} psell={p_sell:.3f} ctx={ctx}")

            conn_a.execute("""
                INSERT INTO ctx_a_latest (instId, ts, score_U, score_A, p_buy, p_sell, ctx)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """, (inst, ts_now, float(u), float(score_A), p_buy, p_sell, ctx))

        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"{inst} error: {e}")

    logging.info("Done.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_ctx_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# SCALP - Dash Contexte A (CTX + Scores + TF Freshness)

import sqlite3
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
import os

DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_OA = "/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"

def connect(path):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return conn

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# LOAD CTX A
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def load_ctx():
    conn = connect(DB_A)
    q = """
        SELECT instId, ts,
               score_U, score_A,
               p_buy, p_sell, ctx
        FROM ctx_a_latest
        ORDER BY instId;
    """
    df = pd.read_sql_query(q, conn)
    conn.close()
    return df

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# FRESHNESS OA
# ---------------------------------------------------------
FRESH_LIMITS = {
    "5m":  300,     # 5 min
    "15m": 900,     # 15 min
    "30m": 1800     # 30 min
}

def load_freshness(tf):
    conn = connect(DB_OA)
    table = f"ohlcv_{tf}"
    q = f"""
        SELECT MAX(ts) as last_ts
        FROM {table};
    """
    row = conn.execute(q).fetchone()
    conn.close()

    if row is None or row[0] is None:
        return None, None, False

    last_ts = row[0]
    age = int(datetime.now().timestamp()*1000 - last_ts) // 1000
    ok = age < FRESH_LIMITS[tf]
    return last_ts, age, ok

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# DISPLAY DASH
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def show():
    os.system("clear")
    print("===== CTX DASH (A) =====\n")

    df = load_ctx()
    
    if df.empty:
        print("CTX vide — A_CTX n'a pas encore tourné.")
        return

    # SUMMARY CONTEXT
    bullish = (df["ctx"] == "bullish").sum()
    bearish = (df["ctx"] == "bearish").sum()
    range_c = (df["ctx"] == "range").sum()
    total   = len(df)

    print("=== CTX SUMMARY ===")
    print(f"bullish | {bullish}")
    print(f"bearish | {bearish}")
    print(f"range   | {range_c}")
    print(f"-------------------")
    print(f"TOTAL   | {total}\n")

    # TOP 5 TRIÉ PAR score_A DESC
    df_sorted = df.sort_values("score_A", ascending=False).head(5)

    print("=== TOP CONTEXTUEL (TOP 5 trié par score_A) ===")
    print(f"{'instId':8} {'ctx':7} {'sU':>5} {'sA':>5} {'pB':>5} {'pS':>5} {'age':>10}")
    print("-"*60)

    now = datetime.now()

    for _, r in df_sorted.iterrows():
        ts = datetime.fromtimestamp(r["ts"] / 1000)
        age = now - ts
        ah = age.seconds // 3600
        am = (age.seconds // 60) % 60
        asec = age.seconds % 60

        print(f"{r['instId']:8} "
              f"{r['ctx']:7} "
              f"{r['score_U']:.2f} "
              f"{r['score_A']:.2f} "
              f"{r['p_buy']:.2f} "
              f"{r['p_sell']:.2f} "
              f"{ah:02d}:{am:02d}:{asec:02d}")


    # FRESHNESS OA
    print("=== LAST OA CANDLES USED ===")
    print(f"{'tf':3} {'last_ts':19} {'age_s':7} {'status'}")
    print("--  -------------------  -------  -------")

    for tf in ["5m", "15m", "30m"]:
        last_ts, age, ok = load_freshness(tf)
        if last_ts is None:
            print(f"{tf:3} {'---':19} {'---':7}  ❌")
            continue

        last = datetime.fromtimestamp(last_ts / 1000).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        status = "✅" if ok else "⚠️"

        print(f"{tf:3} {last:19} {age:7}  {status}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    show()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/A_feat_builder.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# SCALP - A Feature Builder (5m/15m/30m)

import sqlite3
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import logging
import sys

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s A_FEAT %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
        logging.FileHandler("/opt/scalp/project/logs/a_feat_builder.log", mode='a')
    ]
)

def connect_db(path):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

# ---------------------------
# Indicators
# ---------------------------
def compute_indicators(df):
    df = df.sort_values("ts")

    df["ema12"] = df.groupby("instId")["close"].transform(lambda x: x.ewm(span=12).mean())
    df["ema26"] = df.groupby("instId")["close"].transform(lambda x: x.ewm(span=26).mean())
    df["macd"]  = df["ema12"] - df["ema26"]

    def rsi(close):
        delta = close.diff()
        gain = delta.clip(lower=0)
        loss = -delta.clip(upper=0)
        avg_gain = gain.rolling(14).mean()
        avg_loss = loss.rolling(14).mean()
        rs = avg_gain / (avg_loss + 1e-9)
        return 100 - (100 / (1 + rs))

    df["rsi14"] = df.groupby("instId")["close"].transform(rsi)
    return df

# ---------------------------
# Load OHLCV
# ---------------------------
def load_tf(conn, table):
    q = f"""
        SELECT instId, ts, open, high, low, close, volume
        FROM {table}
        ORDER BY instId, ts;
    """
    return pd.read_sql_query(q, conn)

# ---------------------------
# Write FEAT
# ---------------------------
def write_features(conn, df, table):
    conn.execute(f"DELETE FROM {table};")
    out = df[["instId", "ts", "ema12", "ema26", "macd", "rsi14"]]
    out.to_sql(table, conn, if_exists="append", index=False)

# ---------------------------
# MAIN
# ---------------------------
def main():
    logging.info("Start A_FEAT...")

    conn_oa = connect_db("/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db")
    conn_a  = connect_db("/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db")

    TF = {
        "5m":  ("ohlcv_5m",  "feat_5m"),
        "15m": ("ohlcv_15m", "feat_15m"),
        "30m": ("ohlcv_30m", "feat_30m")
    }

    for tf, (ohlcv_table, feat_table) in TF.items():
        logging.info(f"Load {tf} OHLCV…")
        df = load_tf(conn_oa, ohlcv_table)

        if df.empty:
            logging.warning(f"{tf} empty, skip")
            continue

        logging.info(f"Compute indicators {tf}…")
        df = compute_indicators(df)

        logging.info(f"Write {feat_table}…")
        write_features(conn_a, df, feat_table)

    logging.info("A_FEAT completed OK")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_builder.py -----
#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
SCALP — B FEAT BUILDER
FULL REBUILD POUR 1m / 3m / 5m

Schéma feat_xm (26 colonnes strictes) :
instId,ts,o,h,l,c,v,
ema9,ema12,ema21,ema26,ema50,
macd,macdsignal,macdhist,
rsi,atr,
bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width,
mom,roc,slope,ctx
"""

import sqlite3, math, logging

DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_builder.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="[B_FEAT] %(asctime)s → %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
)

# ======================= INDICATEURS ==========================

def ema(prev, price, k):
    return price if prev is None else prev + k*(price-prev)

def compute_rsi(vals, period=14):
    if len(vals) < period+1:
        return None
    gains = losses = 0.0
    for i in range(1, period+1):
        d = vals[-i] - vals[-i-1]
        if d > 0:
            gains += d
        else:
            losses -= d
    if losses <= 0:
        return 100.0
    rs = gains / losses
    return 100.0 - 100.0/(1.0+rs)

def compute_atr(hs, ls, cs, period=14):
    if len(hs) < period+1:
        return None
    trs = []
    for i in range(1, len(hs)):
        tr = max(
            hs[i] - ls[i],
            abs(hs[i] - cs[i-1]),
            abs(ls[i] - cs[i-1])
        )
        trs.append(tr)
    return sum(trs[-period:]) / period

def compute_bb(vals, period=20):
    if len(vals) < period:
        return (None,)*5
    window = vals[-period:]
    mid = sum(window) / period
    var = sum((x-mid)**2 for x in window) / period
    std = math.sqrt(var)
    up  = mid + 2*std
    low = mid - 2*std
    width = (up-low)/mid if mid else None
    return mid, std, up, low, width

# ======================== HELPERS ============================

def fetch_ctx(inst):
    """
    Récupère le dernier ctx calculé par A pour ce coin.
    Si rien, renvoie None.
    """
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        SELECT ctx
        FROM ctx_a_latest
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts DESC
        LIMIT 1;
    """, (inst,))
    row = cur.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return row[0] if row else None

def load_ohlcv(inst, tf):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(f"""
        SELECT ts,o,h,l,c,v
        FROM ohlcv_{tf}
        WHERE instId=?
        ORDER BY ts ASC;
    """, (inst,))
    rows = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return rows

# ====================== FULL REBUILD ==========================

def full_rebuild(inst, tf):
    rows = load_ohlcv(inst, tf)
    if len(rows) < 60:
        return []

    closes = [r[4] for r in rows]
    highs  = [r[2] for r in rows]
    lows   = [r[3] for r in rows]

    ema9 = ema12 = ema21 = ema26 = ema50 = None
    k9 = 2/10; k12 = 2/13; k21 = 2/22; k26 = 2/27; k50 = 2/51

    macd = macdsig = macdhist = None
    ctx_value = fetch_ctx(inst)

    feats = []

    for i, (ts,o,h,l,c,v) in enumerate(rows):

        # EMA
        ema9  = ema(ema9,  c, k9)
        ema12 = ema(ema12, c, k12)
        ema21 = ema(ema21, c, k21)
        ema26 = ema(ema26, c, k26)
        ema50 = ema(ema50, c, k50)

        # MACD
        if ema12 is not None and ema26 is not None:
            macd = ema12 - ema26
            if macdsig is None:
                macdsig = macd
            else:
                macdsig = macdsig*0.9 + macd*0.1
            macdhist = macd - macdsig

        # RSI / ATR / BB
        rsi = compute_rsi(closes[:i+1], 14)
        atr = compute_atr(highs[:i+1], lows[:i+1], closes[:i+1], 14)
        bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width = compute_bb(closes[:i+1], 20)

        # Mom / ROC / slope
        mom = c - rows[i-1][4] if i > 0 else None
        roc = ((c / rows[i-1][4]) - 1.0)*100.0 if i > 0 and rows[i-1][4] else None
        slope = None
        if i > 0 and ema12 is not None and feats:
            prev_ema12 = feats[-1]["ema12"]
            if prev_ema12 is not None:
                slope = ema12 - prev_ema12

        feats.append(dict(
            instId=inst, ts=ts,
            o=o,h=h,l=l,c=c,v=v,
            ema9=ema9, ema12=ema12, ema21=ema21, ema26=ema26, ema50=ema50,
            macd=macd, macdsignal=macdsig, macdhist=macdhist,
            rsi=rsi, atr=atr,
            bb_mid=bb_mid, bb_std=bb_std, bb_up=bb_up, bb_low=bb_low, bb_width=bb_width,
            mom=mom, roc=roc, slope=slope,
            ctx=ctx_value
        ))

    return feats

# ========================= STORE ==============================

def store_full(tf, all_feats):
    if not all_feats:
        return
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur  = conn.cursor()

    # On efface UNE fois par TF
    cur.execute(f"DELETE FROM feat_{tf};")

    cur.executemany(f"""
        INSERT INTO feat_{tf} VALUES (
            :instId,:ts,
            :o,:h,:l,:c,:v,
            :ema9,:ema12,:ema21,:ema26,:ema50,
            :macd,:macdsignal,:macdhist,
            :rsi,:atr,
            :bb_mid,:bb_std,:bb_up,:bb_low,:bb_width,
            :mom,:roc,:slope,:ctx
        );
    """, all_feats)

    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

# ========================= MAIN ===============================

def main():
    logging.info("FULL FEAT REBUILD START")

    # Univers réel depuis OB (coins alimentés)
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    cur  = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT DISTINCT instId FROM ohlcv_1m;")
    insts = [r[0] for r in cur.fetchall()]
    conn.close()

    logging.info(f"UNIVERSE ({len(insts)}) = {insts}")

    for tf in ("1m","3m","5m"):
        all_feats = []
        for inst in insts:
            feats = full_rebuild(inst, tf)
            if feats:
                all_feats.extend(feats)
                logging.info(f"{inst} {tf}: {len(feats)} rows")
            else:
                logging.info(f"{inst} {tf}: NO DATA for {inst} {tf}")
        store_full(tf, all_feats)
        logging.info(f"{tf}: stored {len(all_feats)} rows total")

    logging.info("FULL FEAT REBUILD DONE")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_builder_all.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
SCALP - B_FEAT_BUILDER_ALL
Génération des features EMA/RSI/ATR/Bollinger pour les TF 1m,3m,5m
Sources : ob.db → Destination : b.db
Univers dynamique (u.db)
"""

import sqlite3, pandas as pd, numpy as np, time, logging
from datetime import datetime

DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_U  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
LOG_FILE = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_builder_all.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [B_FEAT_BUILDER] %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG_FILE), logging.StreamHandler()]
)
log = logging.getLogger("B_FEAT_BUILDER")

def connect(db):
    con = sqlite3.connect(db, timeout=10)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return con

def get_universe():
    con = connect(DB_U)
    df = pd.read_sql("SELECT instId FROM universe;", con)
    con.close()
    return [x.replace("/", "") for x in df["instId"].tolist()]

def ema(s, span): return s.ewm(span=span, adjust=False).mean()
def rsi(s, p=14):
    d = s.diff(); up = d.clip(lower=0).rolling(p).mean(); dn = -d.clip(upper=0).rolling(p).mean()
    rs = up / dn; return 100 - (100/(1+rs))
def atr(df, p=14):
    hl = df.h - df.l
    hc = (df.h - df.c.shift()).abs()
    lc = (df.l - df.c.shift()).abs()
    tr = pd.concat([hl, hc, lc], axis=1).max(axis=1)
    return tr.rolling(p).mean()
def boll(df, p=20):
    m = df.c.rolling(p).mean(); s = df.c.rolling(p).std()
    up, lo = m+2*s, m-2*s; w = (up-lo)/m
    return m, s, up, lo, w

def compute(df):
    if df.empty: return df
    df["ema12"]=ema(df.c,12); df["ema26"]=ema(df.c,26)
    df["rsi14"]=rsi(df.c,14); df["atr14"]=atr(df,14)
    df["bb_mid"],df["bb_std"],df["bb_up"],df["bb_low"],df["bb_width"]=boll(df,20)
    return df

def build_tf(tf):
    start=time.time(); con_src=connect(DB_OB); con_dst=connect(DB_B)
    con_dst.execute(f"""CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_{tf} (
        ts INTEGER,o REAL,h REAL,l REAL,c REAL,v REAL,
        ema12 REAL,ema26 REAL,rsi14 REAL,atr14 REAL,
        bb_mid REAL,bb_std REAL,bb_up REAL,bb_low REAL,bb_width REAL,
        instId TEXT);"""); con_dst.commit()
    insts=get_universe(); n=0
    for inst in insts:
        try:
            q=f"SELECT ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE instId='{inst}' ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 500;"
            df=pd.read_sql_query(q,con_src)
            if df.empty: continue
            df=df.sort_values("ts").reset_index(drop=True)
            df=compute(df).dropna()
            if df.empty: continue
            last=df.iloc[-1:].copy(); last["instId"]=inst
            last.to_sql(f"feat_{tf}",con_dst,if_exists="append",index=False)
            n+=1
        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"{inst} {tf}: {e}")
    con_src.close(); con_dst.commit(); con_dst.close()
    log.info(f"{n} instruments mis à jour dans feat_{tf} en {time.time()-start:.2f}s")

def main():
    log.info("→ Démarrage builder (1m/3m/5m)")
    for tf in ["1m","3m","5m"]: build_tf(tf)
    log.info("✅ Terminé")

if __name__=="__main__": main()
