#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
SCALP — B FEAT BUILDER FULL REBUILD
- Rebuild complet des 1m, 3m, 5m depuis OB
- Assure que tous les indicateurs sont sains
"""

import sqlite3, math, logging
from B_feat_builder_incremental import (ema,compute_rsi,compute_bb,compute_atr,fetch_ctx,load_ohlcv,feat_row)

DB_OB="/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B="/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
LOG="/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_builder_full.log"

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG,level=logging.INFO,
    format="[B_FEAT_FULL] %(asctime)s → %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

def full_rebuild(inst,tf):
    rows=load_ohlcv(inst,tf)
    if len(rows)<60: return []

    closes=[r[4] for r in rows]; highs=[r[2] for r in rows]; lows=[r[3] for r in rows]

    ema9=ema12=ema21=ema26=ema50=None
    k9=2/10;k12=2/13;k21=2/22;k26=2/27;k50=2/51

    macd=macdsig=macdhist=None
    ctx=fetch_ctx(inst)
    feats=[]

    for i,(ts,o,h,l,c,v) in enumerate(rows):
        ema9=ema(ema9,c,k9);ema12=ema(ema12,c,k12);ema21=ema(ema21,c,k21)
        ema26=ema(ema26,c,k26);ema50=ema(ema50,c,k50)

        if ema12 and ema26:
            macd=ema12-ema26
            macdsig=macd if macdsig is None else macdsig*0.9+macd*0.1
            macdhist=macd-macdsig

        rsi=compute_rsi(closes[:i+1],14)
        atr=compute_atr(highs[:i+1],lows[:i+1],closes[:i+1])
        bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width=compute_bb(closes[:i+1],20)

        mom=c-rows[i-1][4] if i>0 else None
        roc=((c/rows[i-1][4])-1)*100 if i>0 else None
        slope=ema12-feats[-1]["ema12"] if i>0 and ema12 else None

        feats.append(feat_row(inst,ts,o,h,l,c,v,
            ema9,ema12,ema21,ema26,ema50,
            macd,macdsig,macdhist,
            rsi,atr,bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width,
            mom,roc,slope,ctx))

    return feats

def main():

    insts=[x[0] for x in cur.fetchall()]
    conn.close()

    for inst in insts:
        for tf in ("1m","3m","5m"):
            feats=full_rebuild(inst,tf)
            if not feats:
                logging.info(f"{inst} {tf} SKIP no data")
                continue

            conn=sqlite3.connect(DB_B);cur=conn.cursor()
            cur.execute(f"DELETE FROM feat_{tf}")
            cur.executemany(f"""
            INSERT INTO feat_{tf} VALUES (
            :instId,:ts,:o,:h,:l,:c,:v,
            :ema9,:ema12,:ema21,:ema26,:ema50,
            :macd,:macdsignal,:macdhist,
            :rsi14_1m,:atr14,
            :bb_mid,:bb_std,:bb_up,:bb_low,:bb_width,
            :vol,:mom,:roc,:slope_ema12_1m,:ctx
            );
            """,feats)
            conn.commit();conn.close()

            logging.info(f"{inst} {tf} rebuilt {len(feats)} rows")

    logging.info("END FULL rebuild")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_builder_incremental.py -----
#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
SCALP — B FEAT BUILDER (INCREMENTAL + AUTO-FULL)
Compatible 26 colonnes feat_xm
"""

import sqlite3, math, logging, time

DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_builder.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="[B_FEAT] %(asctime)s → %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
)

# ============================================================
# INDICATEURS
# ============================================================

def ema(prev, price, k): return price if prev is None else prev + k*(price-prev)

def compute_rsi(vals, period=14):
    if len(vals) < period+1: return None
    g = l = 0
    for i in range(1,period+1):
        d = vals[-i] - vals[-i-1]
        if d > 0: g += d
        else:     l -= d
    if l <= 0: return 100
    return 100 - (100/(1+(g/l)))

def compute_bb(vals, period=20):
    if len(vals) < period: return (None,)*5
    s = vals[-period:]
    mid = sum(s)/period
    var = sum((x-mid)**2 for x in s)/period
    std = math.sqrt(var)
    up  = mid + 2*std
    low = mid - 2*std
    width = (up-low)/mid if mid else None
    return mid,std,up,low,width

def compute_atr(hs, ls, cs, period=14):
    if len(hs) < period+1: return None
    trs=[]
    for i in range(1,len(hs)):
        trs.append(max(
            hs[i]-ls[i],
            abs(hs[i]-cs[i-1]),
            abs(ls[i]-cs[i-1])
        ))
    return sum(trs[-period:])/period

# ============================================================
# HELPERS
# ============================================================

def fetch_ctx(inst):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_A)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(
        "SELECT ctx FROM ctx_a_latest WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1",
        (inst,)
    )
    r = cur.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return r[0] if r else None

def last_feat_ts(inst, tf):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_{tf} WHERE instId=?", (inst,))
    r = cur.fetchone()
    conn.close()
    return r[0] if r and r[0] else 0

def load_ohlcv_since(inst, tf, ts_min):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(f"""
        SELECT ts,o,h,l,c,v
        FROM ohlcv_{tf}
        WHERE instId=? AND ts>?
        ORDER BY ts ASC
    """,(inst,ts_min))
    rows = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return rows

# ============================================================
# FULL REBUILD (TF=1m,3m,5m)
# ============================================================

def build_full(inst, tf):
    rows = load_ohlcv_since(inst, tf, 0)
    if len(rows) < 60: return []

    closes=[r[4] for r in rows]
    highs =[r[2] for r in rows]
    lows  =[r[3] for r in rows]

    ema9=ema12=ema21=ema26=ema50=None
    k9=2/10; k12=2/13; k21=2/22; k26=2/27; k50=2/51

    macd=macdsig=macdhist=None
    ctx = fetch_ctx(inst)

    feats=[]

    for i,(ts,o,h,l,c,v) in enumerate(rows):

        ema9  = ema(ema9,  c, k9)
        ema12 = ema(ema12, c, k12)
        ema21 = ema(ema21, c, k21)
        ema26 = ema(ema26, c, k26)
        ema50 = ema(ema50, c, k50)

        if ema12 and ema26:
            macd = ema12 - ema26
            macdsig = macd if macdsig is None else macdsig*0.9 + macd*0.1
            macdhist = macd - macdsig

        rsi = compute_rsi(closes[:i+1], 14)
        atr = compute_atr(highs[:i+1], lows[:i+1], closes[:i+1], 14)
        bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width = compute_bb(closes[:i+1],20)

        mom = c - rows[i-1][4] if i>0 else None
        roc = ((c/rows[i-1][4])-1)*100 if i>0 and rows[i-1][4] else None
        slope = (ema12 - feats[-1]["ema12"]) if i>0 and ema12 else None

        feats.append(dict(
            instId=inst, ts=ts,
            o=o,h=h,l=l,c=c,v=v,
            ema9=ema9, ema12=ema12, ema21=ema21, ema26=ema26, ema50=ema50,
            macd=macd, macdsignal=macdsig, macdhist=macdhist,
            rsi=rsi, atr=atr,
            bb_mid=bb_mid, bb_std=bb_std, bb_up=bb_up, bb_low=bb_low, bb_width=bb_width,
            mom=mom, roc=roc, slope=slope,
            ctx=ctx
        ))

    return feats

# ============================================================
# INCREMENTAL BUILD
# ============================================================

def build_incremental(inst, tf, last_ts):
    rows = load_ohlcv_since(inst, tf, last_ts)
    if not rows:
        return []

    # Charger l’historique existant (EMA, MACD, BB, etc.)
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(f"""
        SELECT ts,o,h,l,c,v,
               ema9,ema12,ema21,ema26,ema50,
               macd,macdsignal,macdhist,
               rsi,atr,
               bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width,
               mom,roc,slope,
               ctx
        FROM feat_{tf}
        WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts ASC
    """,(inst,))
    old = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()

    # Si aucun historique → bascule FULL
    if len(old) < 60:
        return build_full(inst, tf)

    # Derniers états
    last = old[-1]
    ema9,ema12,ema21,ema26,ema50 = last[6],last[7],last[8],last[9],last[10]
    macd,macdsig,macdhist        = last[11],last[12],last[13]
    closes = [r[4] for r in old]  # historique complet
    highs  = [r[2] for r in old]
    lows   = [r[3] for r in old]

    ctx = fetch_ctx(inst)

    feats=[]

    k9=2/10; k12=2/13; k21=2/22; k26=2/27; k50=2/51

    for (ts,o,h,l,c,v) in rows:

        closes.append(c)
        highs.append(h)
        lows.append(l)

        ema9  = ema(ema9,  c, k9)
        ema12 = ema(ema12, c, k12)
        ema21 = ema(ema21, c, k21)
        ema26 = ema(ema26, c, k26)
        ema50 = ema(ema50, c, k50)

        if ema12 and ema26:
            macd = ema12 - ema26
            macdsig = macd if macdsig is None else macdsig*0.9+macd*0.1
            macdhist = macd - macdsig

        rsi = compute_rsi(closes,14)
        atr = compute_atr(highs,lows,closes,14)
        bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width = compute_bb(closes,20)

        mom = c - closes[-2] if len(closes)>1 else None
        roc = ((c/closes[-2]) - 1)*100 if len(closes)>1 and closes[-2] else None
        slope = ema12 - last[7] if ema12 else None

        feats.append(dict(
            instId=inst, ts=ts,
            o=o,h=h,l=l,c=c,v=v,
            ema9=ema9, ema12=ema12, ema21=ema21, ema26=ema26, ema50=ema50,
            macd=macd, macdsignal=macdsig, macdhist=macdhist,
            rsi=rsi, atr=atr,
            bb_mid=bb_mid, bb_std=bb_std, bb_up=bb_up, bb_low=bb_low, bb_width=bb_width,
            mom=mom, roc=roc, slope=slope,
            ctx=ctx
        ))

        last = (ts,o,h,l,c,v,ema9,ema12,ema21,ema26,ema50,macd,macdsig,macdhist,
                rsi,atr,bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width,mom,roc,slope,ctx)

    return feats

# ============================================================
# STORE INCREMENTAL
# ============================================================

def store_incremental(tf, rows):
    if not rows: return
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.executemany(f"""
        INSERT OR REPLACE INTO feat_{tf} (
            instId, ts,
            o,h,l,c,v,
            ema9, ema12, ema21, ema26, ema50,
            macd, macdsignal, macdhist,
            rsi, atr,
            bb_mid, bb_std, bb_up, bb_low, bb_width,
            mom, roc, slope,
            ctx
        ) VALUES (
            :instId, :ts,
            :o,:h,:l,:c,:v,
            :ema9,:ema12,:ema21,:ema26,:ema50,
            :macd,:macdsignal,:macdhist,
            :rsi,:atr,
            :bb_mid,:bb_std,:bb_up,:bb_low,:bb_width,
            :mom,:roc,:slope,
            :ctx
        )
    """, rows)
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

# ============================================================
# MAIN
# ============================================================

def main():
    logging.info("B_FEAT incremental start")

    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_OB)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT DISTINCT instId FROM ohlcv_1m;")
    insts = [x[0] for x in cur.fetchall()]
    conn.close()

    for inst in insts:
        for tf in ("1m","3m","5m"):
            last = last_feat_ts(inst, tf)

            if last == 0:
                feats = build_full(inst, tf)
                if feats:
                    store_incremental(tf, feats)
                    logging.info(f"{inst} {tf} FULL {len(feats)} rows")
                continue

            incr = build_incremental(inst, tf, last)
            if incr:
                store_incremental(tf, incr)
                logging.info(f"{inst} {tf} +{len(incr)} rows")

    logging.info("B_FEAT incremental done")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_feat_full_rebuild.py -----
#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, math, logging

DB_OB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
DB_B  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_A  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_feat_full.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="[B_FEAT_FULL] %(asctime)s → %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
)

def ema(prev, price, k): return price if prev is None else prev + k*(price-prev)

def compute_rsi(vals, period=14):
    if len(vals)<period+1: return None
    g=l=0
    for i in range(1,period+1):
        d=vals[-i]-vals[-i-1]
        if d>0: g+=d
        else:   l-=d
    if l<=0: return 100
    rs=g/l
    return 100 - (100/(1+rs))

def compute_bb(vals, period=20):
    if len(vals)<period: return(None,)*5
    s=vals[-period:]
    mid=sum(s)/period
    var=sum((x-mid)**2 for x in s)/period
    std=math.sqrt(var)
    up=mid+2*std; low=mid-2*std
    width=(up-low)/mid if mid else None
    return mid,std,up,low,width

def compute_atr(hs,ls,cs,period=14):
    if len(hs)<period+1: return None
    trs=[]
    for i in range(1,len(hs)):
        trs.append(max(hs[i]-ls[i],abs(hs[i]-cs[i-1]),abs(ls[i]-cs[i-1])))
    return sum(trs[-period:])/period

def ctx(inst):
    conn=sqlite3.connect(DB_A); cur=conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT ctx FROM ctx_a_latest WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1",(inst,))
    r=cur.fetchone(); conn.close()
    return r[0] if r else None

def build_tf(inst, tf):
    conn=sqlite3.connect(DB_OB); cur=conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(f"SELECT ts,o,h,l,c,v FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts",(inst,))
    rows=cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()

    if len(rows)<60:
        return []

    closes=[r[4] for r in rows]
    highs=[r[2] for r in rows]
    lows=[r[3] for r in rows]

    ema9=ema12=ema21=ema26=ema50=None
    k9=2/10; k12=2/13; k21=2/22; k26=2/27; k50=2/51

    macd=macdsig=macdhist=None
    cctx = ctx(inst)

    feats=[]
    for i,(ts,o,h,l,c,v) in enumerate(rows):

        ema9 = ema(ema9,c,k9)
        ema12= ema(ema12,c,k12)
        ema21= ema(ema21,c,k21)
        ema26= ema(ema26,c,k26)
        ema50= ema(ema50,c,k50)

        if ema12 and ema26:
            macd = ema12 - ema26
            macdsig = macd if macdsig is None else macdsig*0.9 + macd*0.1
            macdhist = macd - macdsig

        rsi=compute_rsi(closes[:i+1],14)
        atr=compute_atr(highs[:i+1],lows[:i+1],closes[:i+1],14)
        bb_mid,bb_std,bb_up,bb_low,bb_width = compute_bb(closes[:i+1],20)

        mom = c - rows[i-1][4] if i>0 else None
        roc = ((c/rows[i-1][4])-1)*100 if i>0 else None
        slope = ema12 - feats[-1]["ema12"] if i>0 and ema12 else None

        feats.append({
            "instId":inst,"ts":ts,"o":o,"h":h,"l":l,"c":c,"v":v,
            "ema9":ema9,"ema12":ema12,"ema21":ema21,"ema26":ema26,"ema50":ema50,
            "macd":macd,"macdsignal":macdsig,"macdhist":macdhist,
            "rsi14_1m":rsi,"atr14":atr,
            "bb_mid":bb_mid,"bb_std":bb_std,"bb_up":bb_up,"bb_low":bb_low,"bb_width":bb_width,
            "vol":v,"mom":mom,"roc":roc,"slope_ema12_1m":slope,"ctx":cctx
        })

    return feats

def store(tf, feats):
    conn=sqlite3.connect(DB_B); cur=conn.cursor()
    cur.execute(f"DELETE FROM feat_{tf}")
    cur.executemany(f"""
    INSERT INTO feat_{tf} VALUES (
    :instId,:ts,:o,:h,:l,:c,:v,
    :ema9,:ema12,:ema21,:ema26,:ema50,
    :macd,:macdsignal,:macdhist,
    :rsi14_1m,:atr14,
    :bb_mid,:bb_std,:bb_up,:bb_low,:bb_width,
    :vol,:mom,:roc,:slope_ema12_1m,:ctx
    )""",feats)
    conn.commit(); conn.close()

def main():
    logging.info("FULL rebuild start")

    conn=sqlite3.connect(DB_OB); cur=conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT DISTINCT instId FROM ohlcv_1m")
    insts=[x[0] for x in cur.fetchall()]
    conn.close()

    for inst in insts:
        for tf in ("1m","3m","5m"):
            feats = build_tf(inst,tf)
            if feats:
                store(tf,feats)
                logging.info(f"{inst} {tf} → {len(feats)} rows")

    logging.info("FULL rebuild end.")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_signals.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, sys, traceback
from datetime import datetime

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    try:
        conn = get_conn()
        cur = conn.cursor()
        cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out(instId,event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        print(f"[SIGNAL] {instId} → {event}", flush=True)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[SIGNAL ERR][bus_notify] {e}", flush=True)

def main():
    print("[SIGNAL] Service started.", flush=True)
    while True:
        try:
            conn = get_conn()
            cur = conn.cursor()
            cur.execute("""
                SELECT id, instId, side, reason, score, ctx, ts
                FROM triggers
                WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-60)*1000
                ORDER BY ts DESC
                LIMIT 50;
            """)
            rows = cur.fetchall()
            n_signals = 0
            for r in rows:
                cur.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO signals_B(instId,side,reason,score_B,ctx,ts_signal)
                    VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?)
                """, (r["instId"],r["side"],r["reason"],r["score"],r["ctx"],r["ts"]))
                bus_notify(r["instId"], "NEW_SIGNAL")
                n_signals += 1
            conn.commit()
            conn.close()
            print(f"[SIGNAL] {datetime.now()} → {n_signals} signaux générés.", flush=True)
            time.sleep(10)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[SIGNAL ERR] {e}", flush=True)
            traceback.print_exc()
            time.sleep(3)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/B_triggers.py -----
#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
SCALP — B_TRIGGERS FULL PRO
10 déclencheurs
Score_B propre à chaque déclencheur
Sélection du meilleur signal par coin
"""

import sqlite3, time, logging, math

DB_B = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
LOG  = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/b_triggers.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="[B_TRIG] %(asctime)s → %(message)s",
    datefmt="%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
)

# ============================================================
# SCORE_B = intensité propre au TRIGGER
# ============================================================

def score_trigger(reason, rsi, slope, macdhist, price, bb_up, bb_low, atr,
                   ema9, ema12, ema21, ema50):

    if reason == "RSI_OVERBOUGHT":
        return max(0, min(100, (rsi-70)*3))

    if reason == "RSI_OVERSOLD":
        return max(0, min(100, (30-rsi)*3))

    if reason == "MOMENTUM_BREAK":
        return max(0, min(100, abs(slope)*8000 ))

    if reason == "MACD_CROSS_UP":
        return max(0, min(100, abs(macdhist)*400 ))

    if reason == "MACD_CROSS_DOWN":
        return max(0, min(100, abs(macdhist)*400 ))

    if reason == "BB_TOUCH_UP" and price and bb_up:
        dist = (price - bb_up) / price
        return max(0, min(100, dist*3000))

    if reason == "BB_TOUCH_LOW" and price and bb_low:
        dist = (bb_low - price) / price
        return max(0, min(100, dist*3000))

    if reason == "ATR_EXPANSION_BREAK" and atr:
        return max(0, min(100, atr * 20))

    if reason == "EMA_STACK_TREND":
        up  = ema9 > ema12 > ema21 > ema50
        dn  = ema9 < ema12 < ema21 < ema50
        return 100 if (up or dn) else 40

    if reason == "RANGE_BREAKOUT":
        return max(0, min(100, abs(slope)*6000))

    return 0


# ============================================================
# LOAD LATEST FEAT
# ============================================================

def fetch_latest():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur  = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        SELECT instId,
               rsi14_1m, slope_ema12_1m,
               macd, macdsignal, macdhist,
               c,
               bb_up, bb_low,
               atr14,
               ema9, ema12, ema21, ema26, ema50,
               ts
        FROM feat_1m
        WHERE ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 900000
        ORDER BY ts DESC
    """)
    rows = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return rows


# ============================================================
# MAIN
# ============================================================

def main():

    rows = fetch_latest()

    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_B)
    cur  = conn.cursor()

    inserted = 0

    for (instId,rsi,slope,macd,macdsig,macdhist,price,
         bb_up,bb_low,atr,ema9,ema12,ema21,ema26,ema50,
         ts) in rows:

        if slope is None or rsi is None:
            continue

        triggers = []

        # =======================================================
        # DÉCLENCHEURS (10)
        # =======================================================

        # 1 RSI OVERBOUGHT
        if rsi>68 and slope<0:
            triggers.append(("sell","RSI_OVERBOUGHT"))

        # 2 RSI OVERSOLD
        if rsi<32 and slope>0:
            triggers.append(("buy","RSI_OVERSOLD"))

        # 3 MOMENTUM BREAK
        if abs(slope)>0.015:
            triggers.append(("buy","MOMENTUM_BREAK") if slope>0 else ("sell","MOMENTUM_BREAK"))

        # 4 MACD CROSS UP
        if macd and macdsig and macd>macdsig and macdhist>0:
            triggers.append(("buy","MACD_CROSS_UP"))

        # 5 MACD CROSS DOWN
        if macd and macdsig and macd<macdsig and macdhist<0:
            triggers.append(("sell","MACD_CROSS_DOWN"))

        # 6 BB TOUCH UP
        if price and bb_up and price>=bb_up:
            triggers.append(("sell","BB_TOUCH_UP"))

        # 7 BB TOUCH LOW
        if price and bb_low and price<=bb_low:
            triggers.append(("buy","BB_TOUCH_LOW"))

        # 8 ATR EXPANSION BREAK
        if atr and ema21 and price:
            if price > ema21 + atr*1.2:
                triggers.append(("buy","ATR_EXPANSION_BREAK"))
            if price < ema21 - atr*1.2:
                triggers.append(("sell","ATR_EXPANSION_BREAK"))

        # 9 EMA STACK TREND
        if ema9 and ema12 and ema21 and ema50:
            if ema9>ema12>ema21>ema50:
                triggers.append(("buy","EMA_STACK_TREND"))
            if ema9<ema12<ema21<ema50:
                triggers.append(("sell","EMA_STACK_TREND"))

        # 10 RANGE BREAKOUT
        if slope and bb_up and bb_low and price:
            mid = (bb_up+bb_low)/2
            up_t   = mid + (bb_up-mid)*1.5
            down_t = mid - (mid-bb_low)*1.5
            if price>=up_t:
                triggers.append(("buy","RANGE_BREAKOUT"))
            if price<=down_t:
                triggers.append(("sell","RANGE_BREAKOUT"))

        if not triggers:
            continue

        # =======================================================
        # SÉLECTION DU MEILLEUR TRIGGER (score_B max)
        # =======================================================

        best_trigger = None
        best_score   = -1

        for side,reason in triggers:
            s = score_trigger(reason, rsi, slope, macdhist, price, bb_up, bb_low,
                              atr, ema9, ema12, ema21, ema50)
            if s > best_score:
                best_score   = s
                best_trigger = (side, reason)

        side,reason = best_trigger

        # anti-duplicate 2 min
        cur.execute("""
            SELECT COUNT(*) FROM triggers
            WHERE instId=? AND side=? AND reason=?
              AND ts > strftime('%s','now')*1000 - 120000;
        """,(instId,side,reason))
        if cur.fetchone()[0]>0:
            continue

        cur.execute("""
            INSERT INTO triggers(instId,side,reason,score,confidence,ts)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """,(instId, side, reason, best_score, best_score/100, int(time.time()*1000)))

        inserted += 1

    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    logging.info(f"{inserted} triggers insérés.")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/H_perf.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, statistics, logging, sys
from pathlib import Path

LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/H_perf.log"
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG), logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)]
)

DB_CLOSED = "/opt/scalp/project/data/x_closed.db"
DB_H = "/opt/scalp/project/data/h.db"

def connect_db(path):
    con = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    con.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    con.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return con

def ensure_closed_schema():
    con = connect_db(DB_CLOSED)
    con.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS positions_closed(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            instId TEXT, side TEXT, entry REAL, exit REAL,
            sl REAL, tp REAL, pnl REAL, reason TEXT,
            ts_open INTEGER, ts_close INTEGER
        )
    """)
    con.close()

def migrate_h():
    con = connect_db(DB_H)
    con.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS score_H(
            instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            avg_pnl REAL,
            winrate REAL,
            trades INTEGER,
            last_update INTEGER
        )
    """)
    con.close()

def compute_score():
    ensure_closed_schema()
    con_c = connect_db(DB_CLOSED)
    rows = con_c.execute("SELECT instId, pnl FROM positions_closed").fetchall()
    con_c.close()
    if not rows:
        logging.info("Aucun trade clos, pas de calcul.")
        return
    data = {}
    for inst,pnl in rows:
        data.setdefault(inst,[]).append(pnl)
    con_h = connect_db(DB_H)
    for inst,vals in data.items():
        avg = statistics.mean(vals)
        winrate = sum(1 for v in vals if v>0)/len(vals)
        con_h.execute("""
            INSERT OR REPLACE INTO score_H(instId,avg_pnl,winrate,trades,last_update)
            VALUES(?,?,?,?,?)
        """,(inst,avg,winrate,len(vals),int(time.time()*1000)))
    con_h.close()
    logging.info(f"Scores H mis à jour pour {len(data)} instruments.")

def main(argv):
    migrate_h()
    compute_score()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv[1:]))

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OA_ohlcv_A.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, ccxt

DBU = "/opt/scalp/project/data/u.db"
DBO = "/opt/scalp/project/data/oa.db"
TF_LIST = ["5m","15m","30m"]
INIT = 150
MAX_ROWS = 300

ex = ccxt.bitget()

def to_bitget_symbol(inst: str) -> str:
    return inst if ":" in inst else f"{inst}:USDT"

def ensure_schema():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBO, timeout=5)
    cur = con.cursor()
    for tf in TF_LIST:
        cur.execute(f"DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ohlcv_{tf}")
        cur.execute(f"""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_{tf}(
          instId TEXT,
          ts INTEGER,
          open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, volume REAL,
          PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
        )
        """)
    con.commit()
    con.close()

def load_universe():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBU, timeout=5)
    rows = [r[0] for r in con.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe")]
    con.close()
    return rows

def last_ts(con, tf, inst):
    row = con.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_{tf} WHERE instId=?", (inst,)).fetchone()
    return row[0] if row and row[0] is not None else None

def upsert_batch(tf, inst, batch):
    if not batch:
        return
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBO, timeout=5)
    cur = con.cursor()
    cur.executemany(
        f"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO ohlcv_{tf}(instId,ts,open,high,low,close,volume) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?)",
        [(inst, o[0], o[1], o[2], o[3], o[4], o[5]) for o in batch]
    )
    cur.execute(f"""
        DELETE FROM ohlcv_{tf}
        WHERE instId=?
          AND ts NOT IN (
            SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_{tf}
            WHERE instId=?
            ORDER BY ts DESC
            LIMIT {MAX_ROWS}
          )
    """, (inst, inst))
    con.commit()
    con.close()

def sync_inst_tf(inst, tf):
    inst_ccxt = to_bitget_symbol(inst)
    con = sqlite3.connect(DBO, timeout=5)
    ts_last = last_ts(con, tf, inst)
    con.close()

    if ts_last is None:
        data = ex.fetch_ohlcv(inst_ccxt, tf, limit=INIT)
        upsert_batch(tf, inst, data)
        return

    data = ex.fetch_ohlcv(inst_ccxt, tf, since=ts_last + 1, limit=150)
    upsert_batch(tf, inst, data)

def main():
    ensure_schema()
    insts = load_universe()
    for inst in insts:
        for tf in TF_LIST:
            try:
                sync_inst_tf(inst, tf)
                time.sleep(0.25)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[OA][{inst}][{tf}] WARN: {e}")
    print("[OA] ✅ Multi-TF sync to oa.db")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OB_collect.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import os, sys, sqlite3, time, logging, subprocess
import ccxt

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_OB = f"{ROOT}/data/ob.db"
DB_U  = f"{ROOT}/data/u.db"
LOG   = f"{ROOT}/logs/ob_collect.log"
FEAT_SCRIPT = f"{ROOT}/scripts/B_feat_builder.py"

# ---------------------------------------------------
# Logging
# ---------------------------------------------------
logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s OB_COLLECT %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)
log = logging.getLogger("OB_COLLECT")

# ---------------------------------------------------
# DB
# ---------------------------------------------------
def connect(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return c

def get_last_ts(conn, table, instId):
    row = conn.execute(
        f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM {table} WHERE instId=?", (instId,)
    ).fetchone()
    return row[0] if row and row[0] else None

# ---------------------------------------------------
# CCXT fetch
# ---------------------------------------------------
def fetch_ccxt(ex, inst, tf, since, limit):
    try:
        return ex.fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=since, limit=limit)
    except Exception as e:
        log.error(f"Fetch error {inst} tf={tf}: {e}")
        return []

# ---------------------------------------------------
# UPSERT
# ---------------------------------------------------
def upsert(conn, table, inst, rows):
    q = f"""
    INSERT INTO {table}(instId, ts, o, h, l, c, v)
    VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
    ON CONFLICT(instId, ts) DO UPDATE SET
        h = MAX(h, excluded.h),
        l = MIN(l, excluded.l),
        c = excluded.c,
        v = excluded.v;
    """
    conn.executemany(
        q, [(inst, r[0], r[1], r[2], r[3], r[4], r[5]) for r in rows]
    )

# ---------------------------------------------------
# Aggregation 3m from tf1 (simple, correct)
# ---------------------------------------------------
def aggregate_3m(conn, inst):
    conn.execute("""
    INSERT INTO ohlcv_3m(instId, ts, o,h,l,c,v)
    SELECT
        instId,
        (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts3,
        FIRST_VALUE(o) OVER w,
        MAX(h) OVER w,
        MIN(l) OVER w,
        LAST_VALUE(c) OVER w,
        SUM(v)  OVER w
    FROM (
        SELECT * FROM ohlcv_1m WHERE instId=? 
    )
    WINDOW w AS (
        PARTITION BY instId, (ts/180000)
        ORDER BY ts
        ROWS BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING
    )
    ON CONFLICT(instId, ts) DO UPDATE SET
        h = MAX(h, excluded.h),
        l = MIN(l, excluded.l),
        c = excluded.c,
        v = excluded.v;
    """, (inst,))

# ---------------------------------------------------
# Purge
# ---------------------------------------------------
def purge(conn, inst):
    conn.execute("""
        DELETE FROM ohlcv_1m
        WHERE instId=? AND ts NOT IN (
            SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_1m 
            WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 450
        );
    """, (inst, inst))

    conn.execute("""
        DELETE FROM ohlcv_3m
        WHERE instId=? AND ts NOT IN (
            SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_3m 
            WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
        );
    """, (inst, inst))

    conn.execute("""
        DELETE FROM ohlcv_5m
        WHERE instId=? AND ts NOT IN (
            SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_5m 
            WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 150
        );
    """, (inst, inst))

# ---------------------------------------------------
# Universe
# ---------------------------------------------------
def universe():
    try:
        c = connect(DB_U)
        rows = c.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe").fetchall()
        c.close()
        return [r[0] for r in rows]
    except:
        return ["BTC/USDT"]

# ---------------------------------------------------
# Main
# ---------------------------------------------------
def main():
    log.info("OB start")

    ex = ccxt.bitget()
    ulist = universe()
    db = connect(DB_OB)

    for inst in ulist:

        # --- 1m ---
        last1 = get_last_ts(db, "ohlcv_1m", inst)
        since1 = last1 + 60000 if last1 else (int(time.time()*1000) - 60000*450)
        raw1 = fetch_ccxt(ex, inst, "1m", since1, 450)
        if raw1:
            upsert(db, "ohlcv_1m", inst, raw1)

        # --- 5m direct ---
        last5 = get_last_ts(db, "ohlcv_5m", inst)
        since5 = last5 + 300000 if last5 else (int(time.time()*1000) - 300000*150)
        raw5 = fetch_ccxt(ex, inst, "5m", since5, 150)
        if raw5:
            upsert(db, "ohlcv_5m", inst, raw5)

        # --- 3m from tf1 ---
        aggregate_3m(db, inst)

        # --- purge ---
        purge(db, inst)

        log.info(f"{inst} new_1m={len(raw1)} new_5m={len(raw5)}")

    db.execute("PRAGMA wal_checkpoint(TRUNCATE);")
    db.close()

    # --- call feat builder ---
    try:
        subprocess.run(
            ["/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3", FEAT_SCRIPT],
            check=True
        )
        log.info("feat built OK")
    except Exception as e:
        log.error(f"feat builder FAIL: {e}")

    log.info("OB done")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        main()
    except Exception as e:
        log.error(f"FATAL {e}")
        sys.exit(1)

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/OB_collect_active.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# coding: utf-8
"""
SCALP - OB_COLLECT (incrémental)
→ Collecte les OHLCV Bitget pour TF 1m et 5m
→ Reconstitue TF 3m à partir de TF1
→ N'insère que les chandelles manquantes
→ Stocke dans ob.db
"""

import os, sys, time, logging, sqlite3, datetime
import ccxt

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db"
LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/ob_collect.log"
EXCHANGE = ccxt.bitget()

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG,
                    level=logging.INFO,
                    format="%(asctime)s OB_COLLECT %(levelname)s %(message)s")

# --- INIT DB ---------------------------------------------------------------
def init_db():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    for tf in ("1m", "3m", "5m"):
        cur.execute(f"""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_{tf} (
            instId TEXT NOT NULL,
            ts INTEGER NOT NULL,
            open REAL, high REAL, low REAL, close REAL, vol REAL,
            PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
        );
        """)
    conn.commit()
    return conn

# --- FETCH OHLCV -----------------------------------------------------------
def fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=None, limit=200):
    try:
        ohlcv = EXCHANGE.fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=since, limit=limit)
        return [(inst, int(c[0]), c[1], c[2], c[3], c[4], c[5]) for c in ohlcv]
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"{inst} {tf} fetch error: {e}")
        return []

# --- BUILD 3M --------------------------------------------------------------
def rebuild_3m(cur):
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM feat_3m;")
    cur.execute("""
        INSERT INTO feat_3m(instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol)
        SELECT instId,
               (ts/180000)*180000 AS ts,
               FIRST_VALUE(open) OVER w AS open,
               MAX(high) OVER w AS high,
               MIN(low) OVER w AS low,
               LAST_VALUE(close) OVER w AS close,
               SUM(vol) OVER w AS vol
        FROM feat_1m
        WINDOW w AS (PARTITION BY instId, (ts/180000) ORDER BY ts ROWS BETWEEN UNBOUNDED PRECEDING AND UNBOUNDED FOLLOWING)
        GROUP BY instId, (ts/180000)
        ORDER BY instId, ts;
    """)

# --- MAIN LOOP -------------------------------------------------------------
def collect_all():
    conn = init_db()
    cur = conn.cursor()

    insts = [
        "BTC/USDT", "ETH/USDT", "SOL/USDT", "LTC/USDT", "BNB/USDT",
        "XRP/USDT", "DOGE/USDT", "ADA/USDT", "DOT/USDT", "LINK/USDT",
        "FIL/USDT", "ICP/USDT", "ATOM/USDT", "TRX/USDT", "AAVE/USDT",
        "BCH/USDT", "ETC/USDT", "UNI/USDT", "XLM/USDT", "XTZ/USDT"
    ]

    total_inserted = 0
    logging.info("start")

    for inst in insts:
        for tf in ("1m", "5m"):
            cur.execute(f"SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_{tf} WHERE instId=?", (inst,))
            ts_max = cur.fetchone()[0]
            since = ts_max + 60_000 if ts_max else None
            rows = fetch_ohlcv(inst, tf, since=since, limit=450 if not ts_max else 2)
            if not rows:
                continue
            cur.executemany(f"""
                INSERT OR IGNORE INTO feat_{tf}(instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?);
            """, rows)
            total_inserted += len(rows)

    rebuild_3m(cur)
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    logging.info(f"done: {total_inserted} rows inserted.")

# --- ENTRYPOINT ------------------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        collect_all()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"FATAL: {e}")

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/T_ticks.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio
import json
import logging
import sqlite3
import time
import websockets

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project"
DB_T = f"{ROOT}/data/t.db"
DB_U = f"{ROOT}/data/u.db"
LOG_FILE = f"{ROOT}/logs/ticks_daemon.log"

logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG_FILE,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s T_TICKS %(levelname)s %(message)s"
)
log = logging.getLogger("T_TICKS")

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# Charger la liste des paires depuis u.db (table universe)
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def load_universe():
    try:
        conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_U, timeout=3)
        rows = conn.execute("SELECT instId FROM universe").fetchall()
        conn.close()
        insts = [r[0].replace("/", "") for r in rows]   # ex: BTC/USDT → BTCUSDT
        return insts
    except Exception as e:
        log.error(f"Cannot load universe: {e}")
        return ["BTCUSDT"]


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# Enregistrement dans t.db
# ---------------------------------------------------------
def save_tick(instId, lastPr, ts):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_T, timeout=2)
    conn.execute("""
    INSERT INTO ticks(instId,lastPr,ts)
    VALUES(?,?,?)
    ON CONFLICT(instId) DO UPDATE SET
        lastPr=excluded.lastPr,
        ts=excluded.ts;
    """, (instId, float(lastPr), int(ts)))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# WebSocket main
# ---------------------------------------------------------
async def run_ws():
    while True:
        insts = load_universe()
        n = len(insts)
        log.info(f"Universe loaded: {n} pairs")

        try:
            async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=10, ping_timeout=10) as ws:

                sub = {
                    "op": "subscribe",
                    "args": [
                        {
                            "instType": "USDT-FUTURES",
                            "channel": "ticker",
                            "instId": s
                        } for s in insts
                    ]
                }

                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
                log.info(f"Subscribed to {n} pairs")

                async for msg in ws:
                    try:
                        data = json.loads(msg)
                        if "data" not in data:
                            continue

                        d = data["data"][0]
                        instId = d["instId"]
                        lastPr = d["lastPr"]
                        ts = d["ts"]

                        save_tick(instId, lastPr, ts)

                    except Exception as e:
                        log.error(f"Tick parse/save error: {e}")

        except Exception as e:
            log.error(f"WS lost, reconnecting: {e}")
            await asyncio.sleep(5)


# ---------------------------------------------------------
# ENTRY POINT
# ---------------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    log.info("T_TICKS starting…")
    asyncio.run(run_ws())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/T_ticks_debug.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio, json, websockets, datetime, re

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"

# liste restreinte pour test
INSTRUMENTS = ["BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT"]

async def listen():
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=20) as ws:
        subs = []
        for inst in INSTRUMENTS:
            subs.append({
                "op": "subscribe",
                "args": [f"ticker:{inst}_UMCBL"]
            })
        for s in subs:
            await ws.send(json.dumps(s))
        print("Subscriptions sent:", subs)

        count = 0
        while True:
            msg = await ws.recv()
            ts = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            print(f"\n[{ts}] RAW:", msg[:200])  # tronqué si long

            # test parsing brut
            try:
                clean = re.search(r'\{.*\}', msg)
                obj = json.loads(clean.group(0)) if clean else None
                if obj:
                    ticker = obj.get("data", [{}])[0]
                    inst = ticker.get("symbol", "?")
                    last = ticker.get("last", "?")
                    print(f"→ Parsed {inst} = {last}")
            except Exception as e:
                print("⚠️ Parse error:", e)

            count += 1
            if count >= 5:
                break

asyncio.run(listen())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/T_ticks_test_raw.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio, json, time, websockets

WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
INSTRUMENTS = ["BTCUSDT", "ETHUSDT", "BNBUSDT"]

async def test():
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=None) as ws:
        subs = [{"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "ticker", "instId": i} for i in INSTRUMENTS]
        msg = {"op": "subscribe", "args": subs}
        await ws.send(json.dumps(msg))
        print("✅ Sent:", msg)

        async def pinger():
            while True:
                await asyncio.sleep(10)
                await ws.send('{"op":"ping"}')
        asyncio.create_task(pinger())

        while True:
            raw = await ws.recv()
            ts = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            print(f"\n[{ts}] RAW →", raw[:250])

            try:
                data = json.loads(raw)
                if "data" in data:
                    for d in data["data"]:
                        inst = d.get("instId")
                        pr   = d.get("lastPr")
                        if inst and pr:
                            print(f"→ Parsed {inst} = {pr}")
            except Exception as e:
                print("⚠️ Parse error:", e)

asyncio.run(test())

import ccxt, sqlite3

        perps.append(inst)

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/b_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time
from datetime import datetime

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
DB_B = "/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db"
DB_T = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

def get_ctx():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_A) as con:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT instId, ctx FROM v_ctx_latest WHERE ctx IN ('bullish','bearish','range');")
        return cur.fetchall()

def get_last_tick(inst):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_T) as con:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT lastPr, ts_ms FROM v_ticks_latest WHERE instId=? LIMIT 1;", (inst,))
        r = cur.fetchone()
    if not r:
        return None, None, None, None
    pr, ts_ms = r
    ts_s = ts_ms / 1000
    hms = datetime.fromtimestamp(ts_s).strftime("%H:%M:%S")
    delta = round(time.time() - ts_s, 1)
    return pr, ts_s, hms, delta

def get_last_signal(inst):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_B) as con:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT ts FROM signals WHERE instId=? ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 1;", (inst,))
        r = cur.fetchone()
    if not r:
        return None, None, None
    ts = float(r[0])
    hms = datetime.fromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M:%S")
    delta = round(time.time() - ts, 1)
    return ts, hms, delta

def dash():
    print(f"===== DASH {datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')} =====")
    for inst, ctx in get_ctx():
        pr, ts_tick, hms_tick, delta_tick = get_last_tick(inst)
        ts_sig, hms_sig, delta_sig = get_last_signal(inst)

        delta = "-"
        if ts_tick and ts_sig:
            delta = round(ts_tick - ts_sig, 1)

        flag = "⚠️" if delta_tick and delta_tick > 5 else "✅"
        print(f"{inst:<10} | ctx={ctx:<8} | price={pr or '-':<10} | "
              f"tick={hms_tick or '-':>8} | sig={hms_sig or '-':>8} | "
              f"Δ={delta:<6} | {flag}")
    print("=" * 90)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    while True:
        try:
            dash()
            time.sleep(3)
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            break
        except Exception as e:
            print("B_DASH ERROR:", e)
            time.sleep(5)

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    print(f"[BUDGET] Event logged: {instId} → {event}")

def main():
    while True:
        print("[BUDGET] Updating exposure / allocation")
        bus_notify("ALL", "BUDGET_UPDATED")
        time.sleep(20)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/budget_updater.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, logging, sys
from pathlib import Path

DB_BUDGET  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db")
DB_OPENER  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db")
DB_CLOSER  = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db")
DB_REC     = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db")
LOG        = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/budget.log"

# -----------------------------------------------------
def setup_logging():
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.INFO,
        format="%(asctime)s BUDGET %(levelname)s %(message)s",
        handlers=[logging.FileHandler(LOG), logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout)],
        force=True,
    )

# -----------------------------------------------------
def connect(path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(path, timeout=30, isolation_level=None)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.execute("PRAGMA busy_timeout=5000;")
    return c

# -----------------------------------------------------
def get_margin_engaged(con_o):
    """Somme de la marge estimée sur les positions ouvertes/pending."""
    try:
        res = con_o.execute("""
            SELECT SUM(entry * qty / leverage)
            FROM trades_open_init
            WHERE status IN ('pending','open');
        """).fetchone()[0]
        return round(res or 0.0, 4)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def get_pnl_real(con_r):
    """Somme du PnL réalisé total depuis l’historique."""
    try:
        res = con_r.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl_net) FROM trades_recorded;").fetchone()[0]
        if res is None:
            res = con_r.execute("SELECT SUM(pnl) FROM trades_recorded;").fetchone()[0]
        return round(res or 0.0, 4)
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

def get_capital_initial(con_b):
    """Capital initial du budget (si non encore présent, crée 1000 USDT)."""
    con_b.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS budget_state(
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id=1),
            balance REAL DEFAULT 1000.0,
            margin REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            pnl_real REAL DEFAULT 0.0,
            ts_update INTEGER
        );
    """)
    con_b.commit()
    row = con_b.execute("SELECT balance FROM budget_state WHERE id=1;").fetchone()
    if not row:
        con_b.execute("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO budget_state(id,balance,margin,pnl_real,ts_update) VALUES (1,1000.0,0.0,0.0,strftime('%s','now'));")
        con_b.commit()
        return 1000.0
    return float(row[0])

# -----------------------------------------------------
def update_budget():
    con_b = connect(DB_BUDGET)
    con_o = connect(DB_OPENER)
    con_r = connect(DB_REC)

    capital = get_capital_initial(con_b)
    margin  = get_margin_engaged(con_o)
    pnl_real = get_pnl_real(con_r)

    new_balance = capital + pnl_real
    ts_now = int(time.time())

    con_b.execute("""
        UPDATE budget_state
        SET balance=?, margin=?, pnl_real=?, ts_update=?
        WHERE id=1;
    """, (new_balance, margin, pnl_real, ts_now))
    con_b.commit()

    con_b.execute("""
        CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_budget_overview AS
        SELECT
            ROUND(balance,4) AS balance,
            ROUND(margin,4)  AS margin,
            ROUND(pnl_real,4) AS pnl_real,
            datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
        FROM budget_state;
    """)
    con_b.commit()

    con_b.close(); con_o.close(); con_r.close()
    logging.info(f"MAJ budget → balance={new_balance:.2f} margin={margin:.2f} pnl_real={pnl_real:.2f}")

# -----------------------------------------------------
def main(_):
    setup_logging()
    logging.info("Budget updater started ✓")
    try:
        update_budget()
    except Exception as e:
        logging.exception(f"Erreur mise à jour budget: {e}")
        raise SystemExit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main(sys.argv[1:]))

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/bus_utils.py -----
import sqlite3, json, time
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

DB_PATH = "/opt/scalp/project/data/bus.db"

def get_conn():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH, timeout=2, isolation_level=None)
    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return conn

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Send a message from one module to another
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_send(source: str, dest: str, stage: str, instId: str, payload: Dict):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        INSERT INTO bus (stage, source, dest, instId, payload)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    """, (stage, source, dest, instId, json.dumps(payload)))
    conn.close()

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Receive unread messages for a given destination + optional stage
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_recv(dest: str, stage: Optional[str] = None) -> List[Dict]:
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    if stage:
        rows = cur.execute("""
            SELECT * FROM bus
            WHERE dest=? AND stage=? AND ack=0
            ORDER BY id ASC
        """, (dest, stage)).fetchall()
    else:
        rows = cur.execute("""
            SELECT * FROM bus
            WHERE dest=? AND ack=0
            ORDER BY id ASC
        """, (dest,)).fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return [dict(r) for r in rows]

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Mark a message as processed
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_ack(msg_id: int):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("UPDATE bus SET ack=1 WHERE id=?", (msg_id,))
    conn.close()

# -------------------------------------------------------------
# Clean acknowledged messages older than N days
# -------------------------------------------------------------
def bus_clean(days: int = 1):
    cutoff = int((time.time() - days * 86400) * 1000)
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("DELETE FROM bus WHERE ack=1 AND ts < ?", (cutoff,))
    conn.close()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, random

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    print(f"[CLOSER] Event logged: {instId} → {event}")

def main():
    insts = ["BTC/USDT", "XRP/USDT", "SOL/USDT"]
    while True:
        inst = random.choice(insts)
        print(f"[CLOSER] Closing {inst}")
        time.sleep(3)
        bus_notify(inst, "CLOSE_DONE")
        time.sleep(7)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/closer_finalize.py -----
import sqlite3, time, logging

DB_FOLLOW = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_CLOSER = "/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db"
DB_REC = "/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"
DB_BUDGET = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"
DB_TICKS = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s CLOSER FIX %(levelname)s %(message)s")

def get_last_price(instId):
    """Récupère le dernier prix connu depuis t.db"""
    try:
        with sqlite3.connect(DB_TICKS) as ct:
            cur = ct.cursor()
            cur.execute("SELECT lastPr FROM v_ticks_latest WHERE instId=? LIMIT 1;", (instId,))
            row = cur.fetchone()
            return float(row[0]) if row else None
    except Exception as e:
        logging.warning(f"{instId}: erreur lecture ticks → {e}")
        return None

def finalize_closures():
    con_f = sqlite3.connect(DB_FOLLOW)
    con_c = sqlite3.connect(DB_CLOSER)
    con_r = sqlite3.connect(DB_REC)
    con_b = sqlite3.connect(DB_BUDGET)

    cur_f = con_f.cursor()
    cur_c = con_c.cursor()
    cur_r = con_r.cursor()
    cur_b = con_b.cursor()

    rows = cur_f.execute("""
        SELECT instId, side, entry, last, qty, reason_close,
               score_U, score_A, score_B, ts_open, ts_update
        FROM trades_follow
        WHERE status='to_close'
    """).fetchall()

    if not rows:
        logging.info("Aucune position à finaliser.")
        return

    for instId, side, entry, last, qty, reason, sU, sA, sB, ts_open, ts_close in rows:
        if last is None:
            last = get_last_price(instId)
            if last is None:
                last = entry
                logging.warning(f"{instId}: aucun prix disponible → fallback entry={entry}")
            else:
                logging.info(f"{instId}: récupéré last depuis ticks = {last}")

        pnl = round((last - entry) * qty * (1 if side == 'buy' else -1), 6)
        logging.info(f"→ CLOSE {instId} {side} pnl={pnl} reason={reason}")

        cur_c.execute("""
            INSERT INTO positions_closed(instId,side,entry,exit,qty,pnl,sl,tp,ts_open,ts_close,reason_exit,score_U,score_A,score_B)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (instId,side,entry,last,qty,pnl,0,0,ts_open,ts_close,reason,sU,sA,sB))

        cur_r.execute("""
            INSERT INTO trades_recorded(instId,side,entry,exit,pnl,reason_exit,ts_open,ts_close,score_U,score_A,score_B)
            VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?)
        """, (instId,side,entry,last,pnl,reason,ts_open,ts_close,sU,sA,sB))

        cur_b.execute("""
            INSERT INTO ledger(src,instId,type,amount,ts)
            VALUES ('closer',?, 'pnl_real', ?, strftime('%s','now')*1000)
        """, (instId, pnl))

        cur_f.execute("UPDATE trades_follow SET status='closed' WHERE instId=?;", (instId,))

    con_c.commit()
    con_r.commit()
    con_b.commit()
    con_f.commit()
    logging.info(f"✓ {len(rows)} clôture(s) finalisée(s).")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    finalize_closures()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/diag_schema.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
"""
diag_schema.py : validation stricte des colonnes contre schema_ref.sql
- Sensible au contexte DB (opener.db / follower.db / closer.db / recorder.db)
- Ignore sqlite_sequence
- Nettoie les commentaires '-- ...' et '/* ... */' avant parsing
- Code retour: 0 si OK, 1 si divergences, 2 si schema_ref absent
Logs: /opt/scalp/project/logs/diag_schema.log
"""
from __future__ import annotations
import re, sys, sqlite3, logging
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/project/data")
SCHEMA_FILE = DATA / "schema_ref.sql"
DBS = [
    ("opener.db",   DATA / "opener.db"),
    ("follower.db", DATA / "follower.db"),
    ("closer.db",   DATA / "closer.db"),
    ("recorder.db", DATA / "recorder.db"),
]

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler("/opt/scalp/project/logs/diag_schema.log"),
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
    ],
)

SectionMap = Dict[str, Dict[str, List[str]]]  # {db_name: {table: [cols...]}}

def _strip_sql_comments(sql: str) -> str:
    sql = re.sub(r"/\*.*?\*/", "", sql, flags=re.S)       # /* ... */
    # Retire les lignes de commentaire -- (en conservant les marqueurs de section)
    cleaned_lines = []
    for line in sql.splitlines():
        if line.strip().startswith("-- ---"):  # garde sections
            cleaned_lines.append(line)
            continue
        if line.strip().startswith("--"):
            continue
        cleaned_lines.append(line)
    return "\n".join(cleaned_lines)

def _split_statements(sql: str) -> List[str]:
    out, buf, depth = [], [], 0
    for ch in sql:
        if ch == "(":
            depth += 1
        elif ch == ")":
            depth = max(depth - 1, 0)
        buf.append(ch)
        if ch == ";" and depth == 0:
            out.append("".join(buf).strip())
            buf = []
    tail = "".join(buf).strip()
    if tail:
        out.append(tail)
    return out

def _extract_cols_from_create(create_sql: str) -> Tuple[str, List[str]]:
    m = re.match(r"(?is)\s*CREATE\s+TABLE\s+(\w+)\s*\((.*)\)\s*;?$", create_sql.strip())
    if not m:
        return "", []
    tname = m.group(1)
    body = m.group(2)

    # Découpe par virgules au niveau 0
    cols_defs: List[str] = []
    token, depth = "", 0
    for ch in body:
        if ch == "(":
            depth += 1
        elif ch == ")":
            depth = max(depth - 1, 0)
        if ch == "," and depth == 0:
            t = token.strip()
            if t:
                cols_defs.append(t)
            token = ""
        else:
            token += ch
    if token.strip():
        cols_defs.append(token.strip())

    cols: List[str] = []
    for cdef in cols_defs:
        s = cdef.strip()
        # ignore contraintes de table
        if re.match(r"(?is)PRIMARY\s+KEY|UNIQUE|CHECK|FOREIGN\s+KEY|CONSTRAINT", s):
            continue
        # prends le premier token comme nom de colonne
        parts = s.split()
        if parts:
            col = parts[0]
            # filtre d'éventuels artefacts comme "--"
            if col != "--":
                cols.append(col)
    return tname, cols

def parse_schema_by_db(schema_text: str) -> SectionMap:
    """
    Parse schema_ref.sql en respectant les sections:
    -- --- opener.db ---   etc.
    Retour: { 'opener.db': {'table': [cols...] , ...}, ... }
    """
    sections: SectionMap = {}
    current = None
    buf = []

    # On garde les sections pour orienter les CREATE TABLE qui suivent
    for line in schema_text.splitlines():
        m = re.match(r"--\s*---\s*([A-Za-z0-9_\.]+)\s*---", line)
        if m:
            # flush précédent
            if current and buf:
                chunk = "\n".join(buf)
                for stmt in _split_statements(chunk):
                    if re.match(r"(?is)\s*CREATE\s+TABLE\s+", stmt):
                        tname, cols = _extract_cols_from_create(stmt)
                        if tname and tname != "sqlite_sequence":
                            sections.setdefault(current, {})[tname] = cols
                buf = []
            current = m.group(1)
            sections.setdefault(current, {})
            continue
        buf.append(line)

    # flush final
    if current and buf:
        chunk = "\n".join(buf)
        for stmt in _split_statements(chunk):
            if re.match(r"(?is)\s*CREATE\s+TABLE\s+", stmt):
                tname, cols = _extract_cols_from_create(stmt)
                if tname and tname != "sqlite_sequence":
                    sections.setdefault(current, {})[tname] = cols

    return sections

def fetch_db_cols(db_path: Path) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
    out: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}
    if not db_path.exists() or db_path.stat().st_size == 0:
        return out
    con = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))
    try:
        cur = con.cursor()
        cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table'")
        for (tname,) in cur.fetchall():
            try:
                cur.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({tname})")
                cols = [r[1] for r in cur.fetchall()]
                out[tname] = cols
            except sqlite3.DatabaseError:
                continue
    finally:
        con.close()
    return out

def main() -> int:
    if not SCHEMA_FILE.exists():
        logging.error("schema_ref.sql introuvable")
        return 2

    raw = SCHEMA_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    cleaned = _strip_sql_comments(raw)
    ref_by_db = parse_schema_by_db(cleaned)

    global_ok = True
    for db_name, db_path in DBS:
        got = fetch_db_cols(db_path)
        if not got:
            logging.warning(f"{db_name}: DB absente ou vide")
            continue

        logging.info(f"--- {db_name} ---")
        ref_tables = ref_by_db.get(db_name, {})

        # compare uniquement les tables présentes dans la REF pour CETTE DB
        for tname, cols_ref in ref_tables.items():
            if tname not in got:
                # table attendue dans cette DB mais absente → signaler
                logging.error(f"{db_name}:{tname} → table manquante")
                global_ok = False
                continue
            cols_got = got[tname]
            miss = [c for c in cols_ref if c not in cols_got]
            extra = [c for c in cols_got if c not in cols_ref]
            if miss or extra:
                global_ok = False
                if miss:
                    logging.error(f"{db_name}:{tname} → colonnes manquantes: {', '.join(miss)}")
                if extra:
                    logging.error(f"{db_name}:{tname} → colonnes en trop: {', '.join(extra)}")

        logging.info(f"{db_name}: CHECK terminé")

    if global_ok:
        print("✅ diag_schema: schéma conforme aux colonnes de schema_ref.sql (par DB)")
        return 0
    else:
        print("❌ diag_schema: divergences détectées (voir logs)")
        return 1

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/follower.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, random, sys, traceback

# force stdout à flusher chaque print immédiatement
sys.stdout.reconfigure(line_buffering=True)

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"

def get_conn():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=5, isolation_level=None)
    conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    conn.execute("PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;")
    return conn

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    try:
        conn = get_conn()
        cur = conn.cursor()
        cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()
        print(f"[FOLLOWER] Event logged: {instId} → {event}", flush=True)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[FOLLOWER ERR][bus_notify] {e}", flush=True)

def main():
    insts = ["BTC/USDT", "ETH/USDT", "ADA/USDT", "SOL/USDT", "XRP/USDT"]
    print("[FOLLOWER] Service started.", flush=True)
    cycle = 0
    while True:
        try:
            cycle += 1
            inst = random.choice(insts)
            pnl = round(random.uniform(-1.5, 1.5), 3)
            print(f"[FOLLOWER] {cycle:04d}  FOLLOW {inst}  pnl={pnl:+.3f}", flush=True)
            bus_notify(inst, "FOLLOW_DONE")
            time.sleep(5)
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\n[FOLLOWER] stopped manually.", flush=True)
            sys.exit(0)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[FOLLOWER ERR][main] {e}", flush=True)
            traceback.print_exc()
            time.sleep(2)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gen_schema_ref.sh -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# -------- CONFIG --------
DATA_DIR="/opt/scalp/project/data"
OUT="${DATA_DIR}/schema_ref.sql"

# -------- INIT --------
{
  echo "-- === SCHEMA GLOBAL SCALP ==="
  echo "-- Généré le $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"
  echo
} > "$OUT"

# -------- EXTRACTION COMPLÈTE --------
for DB in opener.db follower.db closer.db recorder.db; do
  DB_PATH="${DATA_DIR}/${DB}"
  echo "-- --- $DB ---" >> "$OUT"
  if [[ -f "$DB_PATH" ]]; then
    # Sortie complète des tables et vues
    sqlite3 "$DB_PATH" "SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type IN ('table','view') AND sql NOT NULL ORDER BY name;" \
      >> "$OUT" 2>/dev/null || true
    echo >> "$OUT"
  else
    echo "-- (absent) $DB" >> "$OUT"
    echo >> "$OUT"
  fi
done

echo "-- === FIN ===" >> "$OUT"
echo "✅ Schéma complet sauvegardé dans $OUT"

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gest.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3
import logging
import time
import os

# === chemins ===
ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project/data"
DB_G = f"{ROOT}/gest.db"
DB_B = f"{ROOT}/b.db"
LOG = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/gest.log"

# === logging ===
logging.basicConfig(
    filename=LOG,
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s",
)

# === UID stable ===
def make_uid(instId, side, ts_signal):
    return f"T{ts_signal}_{instId.replace('/','')}_{side}"

# === import signaux depuis B ===
def copy_signals_to_trades(limit=500):
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_B) as src, sqlite3.connect(DB_G) as dst:
        src.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
        dst.row_factory = sqlite3.Row

        # Signaux nouveaux uniquement
        rows = src.execute("""
            SELECT b.instId, b.side, b.reason, b.price, b.atr, b.score_B, b.ts_signal,
                   COALESCE(c.ctx,'range') AS ctx
            FROM v_opener_for_gest b
            LEFT JOIN gest.trades_all g
                ON g.instId=b.instId AND g.side=b.side AND g.ts_signal=b.ts_signal
            LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c ON c.instId=b.instId
            WHERE b.price>0 AND g.trade_uid IS NULL
            ORDER BY b.ts_signal DESC
            LIMIT ?
        """, (limit,)).fetchall()

        n_new = 0
        for r in rows:
            t_uid = make_uid(r["instId"], r["side"], r["ts_signal"])
            try:
                dst.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO trades_all(
                        trade_uid, instId, side, reason, ctx,
                        score_B, atr, price, ts_signal,
                        state, ts_create
                    ) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,'NEW',strftime('%s','now')*1000)
                """, (
                    t_uid, r["instId"], r["side"], r["reason"], r["ctx"],
                    r["score_B"], r["atr"], r["price"], r["ts_signal"]
                ))
                n_new += 1
            except sqlite3.IntegrityError:
                continue

        dst.commit()
        if n_new > 0:
            logging.info(f"SYNC {n_new} nouveaux signaux ajoutés")
        return n_new

# === budget ===
def update_budget():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_G) as con:
        pnl_total = con.execute("""
            SELECT COALESCE(SUM(pnl_real),0)
            FROM trades_all
            WHERE state IN ('ACTIVE','CLOSING','CLOSED','RECORDED')
        """).fetchone()[0]
        base_balance = 1000.0
        balance = base_balance + pnl_total
        con.execute("""
            UPDATE budget_state
            SET balance=?, equity=?, margin=0,
                ts_update=strftime('%s','now')*1000
            WHERE id=1
        """, (balance, balance))
        con.commit()
        logging.info(f"BUDGET mis à jour → balance={balance:.2f}")

# === initialisation ===
def init_budget():
    with sqlite3.connect(DB_G) as con:
        con.execute("""
            INSERT OR IGNORE INTO budget_state(id,balance,equity,margin,ts_update)
            VALUES (1,1000,1000,0,strftime('%s','now')*1000)
        """)
        con.commit()

# === boucle principale ===
def main():
    logging.info("GEST pipeline actif (b→gest)")
    init_budget()
    while True:
        try:
            added = copy_signals_to_trades()
            if added > 0:
                update_budget()
            time.sleep(5)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"GEST loop error: {e}")
            time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gest_bus_collector.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import sqlite3, json, time, logging, os

ROOT = "/opt/scalp/project/data"
SRC = {
  "b": f"{ROOT}/b.db",
  "opener": f"{ROOT}/opener.db",
  "closer": f"{ROOT}/closer.db",
}
GEST_DB = f"{ROOT}/gest.db"
LOG_FILE = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/gest_bus.log"

os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(LOG_FILE), exist_ok=True)
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO,
                    format="%(asctime)s GEST_BUS %(levelname)s %(message)s")

def connect(db_path):
    c = sqlite3.connect(db_path, timeout=10, isolation_level=None)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def json_load(s):
    try: return json.loads(s) if s else {}
    except: return {}

def process_row(gcur, row, source):
    inst, event, ts = row["instId"], row["event"], row["ts"]
    payload = json_load(row["payload"] or "{}")
    gcur.execute("INSERT OR IGNORE INTO bus_out(id, src, instId, event, payload, ts, ack) VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,1);",
                 (row["id"], source, inst, event, row["payload"], ts))
    if event in ("NEW_SIGNAL","NEW_TRIGGER"):
        gcur.execute("""INSERT INTO signals_in(instId, side, reason, score, confidence, ctx, ts)
                        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?);""",
                     (inst, payload.get("side"), payload.get("reason"),
                      float(payload.get("score",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("confidence",0) or 0),
                      payload.get("ctx"), ts))
    elif event == "OPEN_DONE":
        gcur.execute("""INSERT INTO trades_all(instId, side, reason, entry, sl, tp, qty, ts_open, status)
                        VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,'open');""",
                     (inst, payload.get("side"), payload.get("reason"),
                      float(payload.get("entry",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("sl",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("tp",0) or 0),
                      float(payload.get("qty",0) or 0), ts))
    elif event == "CLOSE_DONE":
        gcur.execute("""UPDATE trades_all
                        SET pnl=?, ts_close=?, status='closed'
                        WHERE instId=? AND status='open'
                        ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 1;""",
                     (float(payload.get("pnl",0) or 0), ts, inst))

def main():
    logging.info("GEST_BUS démarré")
    gest = connect(GEST_DB); gcur = gest.cursor()
    sources = {n: connect(p) for n,p in SRC.items() if os.path.exists(p)}
    cursors = {n: c.cursor() for n,c in sources.items()}

    while True:
        try:
            total = 0
            for name, cur in cursors.items():
                cur.execute("SELECT id, src, instId, event, payload, ts FROM bus_out WHERE ack=0 ORDER BY id ASC LIMIT 200;")
                rows = cur.fetchall()
                for r in rows:
                    process_row(gcur, r, name)
                    cur.execute("UPDATE bus_out SET ack=1 WHERE id=?;", (r["id"],))
                total += len(rows)
            if total:
                gest.commit()
                for c in sources.values(): c.commit()
                logging.info(f"{total} événements traités.")
            time.sleep(2)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"loop error: {e}")
            time.sleep(5)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/gest_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, os, time
from datetime import datetime

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB, timeout=2)
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def latest_events(cur, limit=15):
    rows = cur.execute("""
        SELECT src, instId, event,
               datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
        FROM bus_events
        ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT ?;
    """, (limit,)).fetchall()
    return rows

def summary(cur):
    rows = cur.execute("""
        SELECT src,
               COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE event LIKE '%DONE%') AS done,
               COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE event LIKE 'NEW%') AS new,
               MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_ts
        FROM bus_events
        GROUP BY src
        ORDER BY src;
    """).fetchall()
    return rows

def main():
    os.system("clear")
    print("===== SCALP BUS DASHBOARD (GEST) =====")
    print(f"{datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print()

    try:
        conn = get_conn()
        cur = conn.cursor()

        srows = summary(cur)
        print("--- SUMMARY ---")
        if not srows:
            print("No data yet.")
        else:
            print(f"{'SRC':<10}{'NEW':>6}{'DONE':>8}{'LAST_EVENT':>22}")
            for r in srows:
                print(f"{r['src']:<10}{r['new']:>6}{r['done']:>8}{r['last_ts']:>22}")
        print()

        rows = latest_events(cur)
        print("--- LATEST EVENTS ---")
        print(f"{'SRC':<10}{'INSTID':<15}{'EVENT':<15}{'TIMESTAMP':>22}")
        for r in rows:
            print(f"{r['src']:<10}{r['instId']:<15}{r['event']:<15}{r['ts_local']:>22}")

        conn.close()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERR] {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        while True:
            main()
            time.sleep(2)
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n[GEST DASH] stopped.")

  side,
  reason,
  'unknown',
  score_B,

  ts_signal

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/health_dash.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import sqlite3, sys
from datetime import datetime

DB_O = "/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
DB_F = "/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db"
DB_BUDGET = "/opt/scalp/project/data/budget.db"

def connect(db):
    con = sqlite3.connect(db)
    con.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return con

def print_table(title, rows):
    print(f"\n--- {title} ---")
    if not rows:
        print("(vide)")
        return
    headers = rows[0].keys()
    print(" | ".join(headers))
    for r in rows:
        print(" | ".join(str(r[k]) for k in headers))

def main():
    print(f"===== PIPELINE HEALTH {datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')} =====")
    co = connect(DB_O)
    cf = connect(DB_F)
    cb = connect(DB_BUDGET)

    print_table("OPEN POSITIONS (opener)", co.execute(
        "SELECT instId, side, status, margin_used FROM trades_open_init ORDER BY ts_open DESC LIMIT 10;"
    ).fetchall())

    print_table("FOLLOW POSITIONS (follower)", cf.execute(
        "SELECT instId, side, status, pnl FROM trades_follow ORDER BY ts_update DESC LIMIT 10;"
    ).fetchall())

    print_table("BUDGET OVERVIEW", cb.execute(
        "SELECT * FROM v_budget_overview;"
    ).fetchall())

    co.close(); cf.close(); cb.close()
    print("\n===== END DASH =====")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
