import sqlite3

DB_A = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"

def init_db():
    con = sqlite3.connect(DB_A, timeout=5)
    cur = con.cursor()

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_5m (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        open REAL,
        high REAL,
        low REAL,
        close REAL,
        vol REAL
    );
    """)

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_15m (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        open REAL,
        high REAL,
        low REAL,
        close REAL,
        vol REAL
    );
    """)

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ohlcv_30m (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        open REAL,
        high REAL,
        low REAL,
        close REAL,
        vol REAL
    );
    """)

    cur.execute("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ctx_a (
        instId TEXT,
        ts INTEGER,
        p_buy REAL,
        p_hold REAL,
        p_sell REAL,
        score REAL,
        ctx TEXT
    );
    """)

    con.commit()
    con.close()
    print("[INIT_DB] OK – A DB ready")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    init_db()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/opener.py -----
#!/opt/scalp/project/venv/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import sqlite3, json, time, logging

DB_BUS   = "/opt/scalp/project/data/bus.db"
DB_OPEN  = "/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db"
LOG_FILE = "/opt/scalp/project/logs/opener.log"

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, level=logging.INFO,
                    format="[OPENER] %(message)s")

def ensure_tables(cur):
    cur.executescript("""
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trades_open_init (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        instId TEXT NOT NULL,
        side TEXT,
        entry REAL,
        sl REAL,
        tp REAL,
        ts_open INTEGER,
        status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
        reason TEXT,
        score REAL,
        confidence REAL DEFAULT 0,
        ctx TEXT,
        ts_create INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000)
    );

    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus_out (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        instId TEXT,
        event TEXT,
        ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
        ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        payload TEXT DEFAULT '{}'
    );
    """)

def fetch_new_signals():
    """Lit les signaux du bus central stage=B → dest=opener."""
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_BUS)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        SELECT instId, payload
        FROM bus
        WHERE stage='B'
          AND dest='opener'
          AND ack=0
          AND ts > (strftime('%s','now')-60)*1000
        ORDER BY ts DESC;
    """)
    rows = cur.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    return rows

def mark_ack(instId):
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_BUS)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("UPDATE bus SET ack=1 WHERE dest='opener' AND instId=?;", (instId,))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

def open_trade(cur, instId, side, reason, score, conf, ctx):
    ts_open = int(time.time()*1000)
    cur.execute("""
        INSERT INTO trades_open_init
        (instId, side, entry, sl, tp, ts_open, status, reason, score, confidence, ctx)
        VALUES (?, ?, 0, 0, 0, ?, 'open', ?, ?, ?, ?);
    """, (instId, side, ts_open, reason, score, conf, ctx))

    cur.execute("""
        INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event, payload)
        VALUES (?, 'OPEN_DONE',
                json_object('side', ?, 'reason', ?, 'score', ?, 'confidence', ?, 'ctx', ?));
    """, (instId, side, reason, score, conf, ctx))

def main():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_OPEN)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    ensure_tables(cur)

    signals = fetch_new_signals()
    n = 0
    for instId, payload in signals:
        try:
            data = json.loads(payload or "{}")
            side  = data.get("side", "buy")
            reason = data.get("reason", "")
            score  = float(data.get("score", 0))
            conf   = float(data.get("confidence", 0))
            ctx    = data.get("ctx", "range")
            open_trade(cur, instId, side, reason, score, conf, ctx)
            mark_ack(instId)
            logging.info(f"{instId} opened ({side})")
            n += 1
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"{instId} error: {e}")

    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    logging.info(f"{n} trades ouverts.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/recorder.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sqlite3, time, random

DB = "/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db"

def get_conn():
    c = sqlite3.connect(DB)
    c.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;")
    c.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    return c

def bus_notify(instId, event):
    conn = get_conn()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("INSERT INTO bus_out (instId, event) VALUES (?,?)", (instId, event))
    conn.commit()
    conn.close()
    print(f"[RECORDER] Event logged: {instId} → {event}")

def main():
    insts = ["BTC/USDT", "ETH/USDT", "SOL/USDT"]
    while True:
        inst = random.choice(insts)
        print(f"[RECORDER] Recording {inst}")
        time.sleep(2)
        bus_notify(inst, "RECORD_DONE")
        time.sleep(10)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import asyncio, json, websockets, datetime

URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

async def main():
    sub = {
        "op": "subscribe",
        "args": [
            {
                "instType": "USDT-FUTURES",
                "channel": "candle1m",
                "instId": "BTCUSDT"
            }
        ]
    }
    async with websockets.connect(URL, ping_interval=20) as ws:
        print("✅ Connected to Bitget WS v2")
        await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
        print("📡 Subscription sent:")
        print(json.dumps(sub, indent=2))
        print("\n--- Waiting for messages ---\n")
        # Display first 5 real messages received
        count = 0
        while count < 5:
            raw = await ws.recv()
            data = json.loads(raw)
            ts = datetime.datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M:%S")
            print(f"[{ts}] {data}")
            count += 1

asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, websockets, time

async def main():
    url = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"
    payload = {
        "op": "subscribe",
        "args": [{
            "instType": "USDT-FUTURES",
            "channel": "ticker",
            "instId": "BTCUSDT"
        }]
    }

    print("Connecting to Bitget WS...")
    async with websockets.connect(url, ping_interval=20) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(payload))
        print("Subscribed to BTCUSDT ticker (USDT-FUTURES)\n")

        async for msg in ws:
            data = json.loads(msg)
            if "data" in data:
                tick = data["data"][0]
                price = tick.get("lastPr")
                ts = tick.get("ts")
                if price:
                    print(f"[{time.strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] BTCUSDT -> {price} (ts={ts})")

asyncio.run(main())

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/scripts/ticks.py -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import asyncio
import json
import sqlite3
import threading
import time
from queue import Queue
import websockets

DB_PATH = "/opt/scalp/project/data/t.db"
DB_A_PATH = "/opt/scalp/project/data/a.db"
WS_URL = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"
FLUSH_INTERVAL = 0.5  # secondes
QUEUE_MAX = 5000

q = Queue(maxsize=QUEUE_MAX)
lock = threading.Lock()
stop_event = threading.Event()

# --- Connexion SQLite optimisée ---
def init_db():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_PATH, check_same_thread=False, timeout=10)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.executescript("""
        PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
        PRAGMA synchronous=OFF;
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ticks(
            instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            price REAL,
            ts_ms INTEGER
        );
        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_ticks_ts ON ticks(ts_ms);
    """)
    conn.commit()
    return conn

# --- Récupération des symboles depuis le contexte A ---
def get_symbols():
    conn = sqlite3.connect(DB_A_PATH)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("SELECT instId FROM v_ctx_latest;")
    symbols = [r[0].replace("/", "") for r in cur.fetchall()]
    conn.close()
    return symbols

# --- Thread d'écriture SQLite ---
def writer_thread():
    conn = init_db()
    cur = conn.cursor()
    last_flush = 0
    buffer = []
    while not stop_event.is_set():
        try:
            tick = q.get(timeout=FLUSH_INTERVAL)
            buffer.append(tick)
        except:
            pass

        now = time.time()
        if now - last_flush >= FLUSH_INTERVAL and buffer:
            with lock:
                cur.executemany(
                    "INSERT INTO ticks (instId, price, ts_ms) VALUES (?, ?, ?) "
                    "ON CONFLICT(instId) DO UPDATE SET price=excluded.price, ts_ms=excluded.ts_ms;",
                    buffer,
                )
                conn.commit()
                buffer.clear()
                last_flush = now

    conn.commit()
    conn.close()

# --- Fonction WS principale ---
async def ws_consumer():
    symbols = get_symbols()
    args = [
        {"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "ticker", "instId": s}
        for s in symbols
    ]
    sub_msg = json.dumps({"op": "subscribe", "args": args})
    print(f"[ticks] Subscribing to {len(symbols)} symbols...")

    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=15, ping_timeout=10) as ws:
        await ws.send(sub_msg)
        print("[ticks] Connected & subscribed.")
        async for msg in ws:
            data = json.loads(msg)
            if "data" not in data:
                continue
            for d in data["data"]:
                try:
                    instId = d["instId"]
                    price = float(d["lastPr"])
                    ts_ms = int(d["ts"])
                    if not q.full():
                        q.put((instId, price, ts_ms))
                except Exception as e:
                    pass

# --- Main ---
def main():
    wt = threading.Thread(target=writer_thread, daemon=True)
    wt.start()

    try:
        asyncio.run(ws_consumer())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("Stopping...")
    finally:
        stop_event.set()
        wt.join()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/A_ctx.sql -----
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_A_latest;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_A_features;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ctx_a_latest;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ctx_a_latest (
    instId TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    ts INTEGER,
    score_U REAL,
    score_A REAL,
    p_buy REAL,
    p_hold REAL,
    p_sell REAL,
    ctx TEXT
);

-- vue features multi-TF (inputs pour le modèle NEUTRAL)
CREATE VIEW v_A_features AS
SELECT
    m5.instId AS instId,
    m5.close AS close_5m,
    m15.close AS close_15m,
    m30.close AS close_30m,
    m5.ts AS ts
FROM ohlcv_5m m5
JOIN ohlcv_15m m15 ON m15.instId=m5.instId
JOIN ohlcv_30m m30 ON m30.instId=m5.instId;

-- vue sortie finale
CREATE VIEW v_A_latest AS
SELECT *
FROM ctx_a_latest;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/a_ctx.sql -----
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS ctx_a_latest;

CREATE VIEW ctx_a_latest AS
SELECT 
    f30.instId,
    f30.ts,
    COALESCE((ABS(f5.macd) + ABS(f15.macd) + ABS(f30.macd)) / 3.0, 0) AS score_A,
    CASE
        WHEN f5.macd > 0 AND f15.macd > 0 AND f30.macd > 0 THEN 'bullish'
        WHEN f5.macd < 0 AND f15.macd < 0 AND f30.macd < 0 THEN 'bearish'
        ELSE 'range'
    END AS ctx
FROM ohlcv_30m f30
LEFT JOIN ohlcv_15m f15 ON f15.instId=f30.instId
LEFT JOIN ohlcv_5m  f5  ON f5.instId=f30.instId
WHERE f30.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_30m f3 WHERE f3.instId=f30.instId)
GROUP BY f30.instId;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/a_ctx_fix.sql -----
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS ctx_a_latest;

CREATE VIEW ctx_a_latest AS
SELECT a1.instId, a1.ts, a1.score_U, a1.score_A, a1.p_buy, a1.p_sell, a1.ctx
FROM ctx_A a1
WHERE a1.ts = (
    SELECT MAX(a2.ts)
    FROM ctx_A a2
    WHERE a2.instId = a1.instId
);

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/a_schema.sql -----
-- =========================================================
-- SCHEMA A : contextes multi-TF
-- =========================================================

-- --- tables brutes importées depuis OA ---
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_5m;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_15m;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_30m;

CREATE TABLE feat_5m AS
SELECT instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol FROM main.ohlcv_5m;

CREATE TABLE feat_15m AS
SELECT instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol FROM main.ohlcv_15m;

CREATE TABLE feat_30m AS
SELECT instId, ts, open, high, low, close, vol FROM main.ohlcv_30m;

-- --- Ajout colonnes d'indicateurs ---
ALTER TABLE feat_5m  ADD COLUMN ema12 REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_5m  ADD COLUMN ema26 REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_5m  ADD COLUMN macd  REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_5m  ADD COLUMN rsi14 REAL;

ALTER TABLE feat_15m ADD COLUMN ema12 REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_15m ADD COLUMN ema26 REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_15m ADD COLUMN macd  REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_15m ADD COLUMN rsi14 REAL;

ALTER TABLE feat_30m ADD COLUMN ema12 REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_30m ADD COLUMN ema26 REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_30m ADD COLUMN macd  REAL;
ALTER TABLE feat_30m ADD COLUMN rsi14 REAL;

-- --- Table des contextes ---
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS ctx_A;
CREATE TABLE ctx_A (
    instId   TEXT,
    ts       INTEGER,
    score_U  REAL,
    score_A  REAL,
    p_buy    REAL,
    p_sell   REAL,
    ctx      TEXT
);

-- --- Vue simplifiée du dernier contexte ---
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS ctx_a_latest;
CREATE VIEW ctx_a_latest AS
SELECT instId, ts, score_U, score_A, p_buy, p_sell, ctx
FROM ctx_A
WHERE ts = (SELECT MAX(ts2) FROM ctx_A t2 WHERE t2.instId = ctx_A.instId);

-- === TABLE SIGNALS_B ===
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,
    reason TEXT,
    price REAL,
    ctx TEXT,
    score_A REAL DEFAULT 0,
    score_B REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ts INTEGER,
    ts_hms TEXT
);

-- === VIEW v_signals_latest ===
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_signals_latest;
CREATE VIEW v_signals_latest AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    price,
    ctx,
    score_A,
    score_B,
    datetime(ts, 'unixepoch', 'localtime') AS ts_hms,
    printf('%02d:%02d', (strftime('%s','now') - ts)/60, (strftime('%s','now') - ts)%60) AS age_hms
FROM signals_B
ORDER BY ts DESC;

-- === VIEW v_for_opener ===
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_opener;
CREATE VIEW v_for_opener AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    reason AS entry_reason,
    price AS price_signal,
    ctx,
    score_A,
    score_B,
    ts,
    ts_hms
FROM v_signals_latest
WHERE score_B >= 70
ORDER BY ts DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/b_v_atr_latest_flat.sql -----
-- Vue: v_atr_latest_flat (instId sans '/'), ts, atr
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_atr_latest_flat;
CREATE VIEW v_atr_latest_flat AS
WITH latest AS (
  SELECT instId, MAX(ts) AS ts
  FROM feat_1m
  GROUP BY instId
)
SELECT
  REPLACE(f.instId,'/','') AS instId,
  f.ts,
  f.atr
FROM feat_1m f
JOIN latest l
  ON f.instId = l.instId AND f.ts = l.ts;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/b_view_for_opener.sql -----
-- Vue de production pour opener, compatible avec version actuelle de B
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_opener;
CREATE VIEW v_for_opener AS
SELECT
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER () AS id,
    instId,
    side,
    reason AS entry_reason,    -- MR, BO, PB, REV, CONT, RNG
    NULL AS score_U,           -- réservé pour score univers
    score_A,                   -- score actuel émis par B
    NULL AS score_B,           -- réservé pour score signal B
    price,
    ts * 1000 AS ts_signal     -- alignement ms
FROM v_signals_latest
WHERE side IN ('buy','sell');

       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open_local,
       CASE WHEN ts_close>0 THEN datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') END AS ts_close_local,
       round(pnl,4) AS pnl
FROM trades_all
ORDER BY ts_open DESC;

       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open_local,

FROM trades_all
ORDER BY ts_open DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/gest_triggers.sql -----
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/opener.db' AS opener;
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/follower.db' AS follower;
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/closer.db' AS closer;
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/recorder.db' AS recorder;

-- Lorsqu’un signal est reçu, on pousse vers opener
CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS trg_gest_to_opener
AFTER INSERT ON bus_events
WHEN NEW.event='NEW_SIGNAL'
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO opener.to_open (instId, ts_create)
    VALUES (NEW.instId, strftime('%s','now')*1000);
END;

-- Lorsqu’un opener envoie confirmation
CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS trg_opener_to_follower
AFTER INSERT ON bus_events
WHEN NEW.event='OPEN_DONE'
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO follower.to_follow (instId, ts_create)
    VALUES (NEW.instId, strftime('%s','now')*1000);
END;

-- Idem pour closer
CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS trg_follower_to_closer
AFTER INSERT ON bus_events
WHEN NEW.event='FOLLOW_DONE'
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO closer.to_close (instId, ts_create)
    VALUES (NEW.instId, strftime('%s','now')*1000);
END;

-- Et recorder
CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS trg_closer_to_recorder
AFTER INSERT ON bus_events
WHEN NEW.event='CLOSE_DONE'
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO recorder.to_record (instId, ts_create)
    VALUES (NEW.instId, strftime('%s','now')*1000);
END;

DETACH DATABASE opener;
DETACH DATABASE follower;
DETACH DATABASE closer;
DETACH DATABASE recorder;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/h_view.sql -----
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_latest;
CREATE VIEW v_H_latest AS
WITH last20 AS (
    SELECT pnl, pnl_pct
    FROM history
    ORDER BY ts_close DESC
    LIMIT 20
),
stats AS (
    SELECT 
        (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM last20 WHERE pnl > 0) * 1.0 / (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM last20) AS winrate,
        (SELECT SUM(pnl) FROM last20 WHERE pnl > 0) AS sum_win,
        (SELECT SUM(ABS(pnl)) FROM last20 WHERE pnl < 0) AS sum_loss
)
SELECT 
    winrate,
    CASE WHEN sum_loss IS NULL OR sum_loss=0 THEN 1.0 ELSE MIN(1.0, (sum_win / sum_loss) / 2.0) END AS pf_norm,
    (0.50*winrate + 0.50*CASE WHEN sum_loss IS NULL OR sum_loss=0 THEN 1.0 ELSE MIN(1.0, (sum_win / sum_loss) / 2.0) END) AS score_H
FROM stats;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/init_b.sql -----
-- ===============================
-- SCHEMA INIT pour b.db (BUS V2)
-- ===============================

PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;

-- Table des déclencheurs bruts
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS triggers (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    tf TEXT DEFAULT '1m',
    side TEXT CHECK(side IN ('buy','sell')),
    reason TEXT,
    score REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ctx TEXT,
    ts INTEGER NOT NULL
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_triggers_inst ON triggers(instId);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_triggers_ts ON triggers(ts);

-- Table des signaux consolidés
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS signals_B (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT NOT NULL,
    side TEXT CHECK(side IN ('buy','sell')),
    reason TEXT,
    score_B REAL,
    ctx TEXT,
    ts_signal INTEGER
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_signalsB_inst ON signals_B(instId);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_signalsB_ts ON signals_B(ts_signal);

-- Bus de sortie pour communication vers gest
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus_out (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT,
    event TEXT,
    ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
    ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_out_ts ON bus_out(ts);

-- ============================================
-- Vue de synthèse pour monitoring des signaux
-- ============================================
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_signals_overview AS
SELECT
    s.instId,
    s.side,
    s.reason,
    s.score_B,
    s.ctx,
    datetime(s.ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
    ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - s.ts_signal)/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM signals_B s
WHERE s.ts_signal = (
    SELECT MAX(ts_signal)
    FROM signals_B s2
    WHERE s2.instId = s.instId
);

PRAGMA foreign_keys = OFF;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_1m;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_3m;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_1m (
    instId      TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts          INTEGER NOT NULL,

    -- OHLCV
    o           REAL,
    h           REAL,
    l           REAL,
    c           REAL,
    v           REAL,

    -- EMA family
    ema9        REAL,
    ema12       REAL,
    ema21       REAL,
    ema26       REAL,
    ema50       REAL,

    -- MACD
    macd        REAL,
    macdsignal  REAL,
    macdhist    REAL,

    -- RSI
    rsi14_1m    REAL,

    -- ATR
    atr14       REAL,

    -- Bollinger Bands
    bb_mid      REAL,
    bb_std      REAL,
    bb_up       REAL,
    bb_low      REAL,
    bb_width    REAL,

    -- Other indicators Full Pro
    vol         REAL,
    mom         REAL,
    roc         REAL,

    -- Derived
    slope_ema12_1m REAL,

    -- Context
    ctx         TEXT CHECK(ctx IN ('bullish','bearish','range')),

    PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_5m AS SELECT * FROM feat_1m WHERE 0;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/init_bus_central.sql -----
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bus (
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  stage TEXT,           -- 'B','O','F','C','R','budget', etc.
  source TEXT,          -- module source (signal, opener, follower, closer, recorder, budget)
  dest TEXT,            -- destinataire
  instId TEXT,
  payload TEXT DEFAULT '{}',
  ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
  ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_stage_dest_ack ON bus(stage, dest, ack, ts);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_bus_ts ON bus(ts);

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/init_bus_out.sql -----

CREATE TABLE bus_out (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    src TEXT,
    instId TEXT,
    event TEXT,
    payload TEXT,
    ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_bus_src   ON bus_out(src);
CREATE INDEX idx_bus_event ON bus_out(event);
CREATE INDEX idx_bus_ts    ON bus_out(ts);

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/init_macd.sql -----
-- =========================================================
-- Calcule basique MACD sur les trois TF
-- =========================================================

UPDATE ohlcv_5m
SET macd = (SELECT close - AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_5m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_5m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_5m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 26));

UPDATE ohlcv_15m
SET macd = (SELECT close - AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_15m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_15m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_15m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 26));

UPDATE ohlcv_30m
SET macd = (SELECT close - AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_30m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_30m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_30m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 26));

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/migrate_bus_out_all.sql -----
-- Idempotent migration: ensure bus_out has src, payload, ack

-- Helper: add column if missing (no-op if exists)
-- (SQLite: we'll attempt ADD COLUMN; if exists it'll error; ignore errors with ';')

/* b.db (signal) */
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/b.db' AS bdb;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS bdb.bus_out (
  id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
  src TEXT,
  instId TEXT,
  event TEXT,
  payload TEXT DEFAULT '{}',
  ts INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
  ack INTEGER DEFAULT 0
);
-- Try to add missing columns (errors ignored)
ALTER TABLE bdb.bus_out ADD COLUMN src TEXT;         -- if missing

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/migrate_feat_full.sql -----
-- =====================================================
-- SCALP — MIGRATION FULL PRO (feat_1m / feat_3m / feat_5m)
-- Nicolas - version OFCR Full Pro
-- Idempotent, propre, conforme guidelines IA
-- =====================================================

PRAGMA foreign_keys = OFF;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_1m;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_3m;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_5m;

-- =====================================================
-- TABLE TEMPLATE (Full Pro)
-- =====================================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_1m (
    instId      TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts          INTEGER NOT NULL,

    -- Price
    o           REAL,
    h           REAL,
    l           REAL,
    c           REAL,
    v           REAL,

    -- EMA
    ema9        REAL,
    ema12       REAL,
    ema21       REAL,
    ema26       REAL,
    ema50       REAL,

    -- MACD
    macd        REAL,
    macdsignal  REAL,
    macdhist    REAL,

    -- RSI
    rsi14_1m    REAL,

    -- ATR
    atr14       REAL,

    -- Bollinger
    bb_mid      REAL,
    bb_std      REAL,
    bb_up       REAL,
    bb_low      REAL,
    bb_width    REAL,

    -- Other indicators Full Pro
    vol         REAL,
    mom         REAL,
    roc         REAL,

    -- Derived
    slope_ema12_1m REAL,

    -- ctx intégré FullPro
    ctx         TEXT CHECK(ctx IN ('bullish','bearish','range')),

    PRIMARY KEY(instId, ts)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_3m   AS SELECT * FROM feat_1m WHERE 0;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS feat_5m   AS SELECT * FROM feat_1m WHERE 0;

PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON;

-- OA INDICATORS (EMA, RSI, MACD, STOCH, ATR)
-- Corrigé pour tables: ohlcv_5m / ohlcv_15m / ohlcv_30m

-- EMA simple proxy (SMA initiale)
UPDATE ohlcv_5m
SET ema12 = (SELECT AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_5m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_5m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_5m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 12)),
    ema26 = (SELECT AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_5m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_5m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_5m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 26));
UPDATE ohlcv_5m SET macd = ema12 - ema26;

UPDATE ohlcv_15m
SET ema12 = (SELECT AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_15m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_15m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_15m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 12)),
    ema26 = (SELECT AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_15m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_15m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_15m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 26));
UPDATE ohlcv_15m SET macd = ema12 - ema26;

UPDATE ohlcv_30m
SET ema12 = (SELECT AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_30m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_30m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_30m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 12)),
    ema26 = (SELECT AVG(close) FROM (SELECT close FROM ohlcv_30m o2 WHERE o2.instId=ohlcv_30m.instId AND o2.ts<=ohlcv_30m.ts ORDER BY ts DESC LIMIT 26));
UPDATE ohlcv_30m SET macd = ema12 - ema26;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/ob_views.sql -----
PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous=NORMAL;

------------------------------------------------------------
-- Vue 1 : v_feat_latest
-- Dernière bougie (close, ts_local, TF) par instrument
------------------------------------------------------------
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_feat_latest;
CREATE VIEW v_feat_latest AS
SELECT '1m' AS tf,
       f1.instId,
       f1.close,
       f1.ts,
       datetime(f1.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
  FROM feat_1m f1
 WHERE f1.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_1m f2 WHERE f2.instId=f1.instId)
UNION ALL
SELECT '3m', f3.instId, f3.close, f3.ts,
       datetime(f3.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
  FROM feat_3m f3
 WHERE f3.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_3m f4 WHERE f4.instId=f3.instId)
UNION ALL
SELECT '5m', f5.instId, f5.close, f5.ts,
       datetime(f5.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
  FROM feat_5m f5
 WHERE f5.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_5m f6 WHERE f6.instId=f5.instId);

------------------------------------------------------------
-- Vue 2 : v_feat_overview
-- Synthèse multi-TF : close1m, close3m, close5m, ema et RSI
------------------------------------------------------------
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_feat_overview;
CREATE VIEW v_feat_overview AS
SELECT f1.instId,
       f1.close AS close_1m,
       f3.close AS close_3m,
       f5.close AS close_5m,
       f1.ema12 AS ema12_1m,
       f3.ema12 AS ema12_3m,
       f5.ema12 AS ema12_5m,
       f1.ema26 AS ema26_1m,
       f3.ema26 AS ema26_3m,
       f5.ema26 AS ema26_5m,
       f1.rsi14 AS rsi14_1m,
       f3.rsi14 AS rsi14_3m,
       f5.rsi14 AS rsi14_5m,
       f1.ts AS ts_1m,
       f3.ts AS ts_3m,
       f5.ts AS ts_5m,
       datetime(f1.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local_1m,
       datetime(f3.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local_3m,
       datetime(f5.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local_5m
  FROM feat_1m f1
  LEFT JOIN feat_3m f3 ON f3.instId=f1.instId
  LEFT JOIN feat_5m f5 ON f5.instId=f1.instId
 WHERE f1.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_1m f WHERE f.instId=f1.instId)
   AND f3.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_3m f WHERE f.instId=f3.instId)
   AND f5.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_5m f WHERE f.instId=f5.instId);

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/ofcr_follower_migrate.sql -----
-- FOLLOWER
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS trades_follow (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT, side TEXT,
    entry REAL, sl REAL, tp REAL, atr REAL,
    pnl REAL DEFAULT 0, last REAL, atr_current REAL,
    ctx TEXT, score_B REAL,
    ts_open INTEGER,     -- hérité de l’opener
    ts_update INTEGER,   -- heartbeat follower
    status TEXT DEFAULT 'active',
    exit_reason TEXT
);

-- Vue attendue par closer : expose ts_follow = ts_update
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_for_close;
CREATE VIEW v_for_close AS
SELECT
    instId, side, entry,
    last, sl, tp, atr_current,
    ts_update AS ts_follow
FROM trades_follow
WHERE status='to_close';

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/rebuild_feat_1m.sql -----
-- ============================================================
-- Rebuild complet de la table feat_1m (structure standard SCALP)
-- ============================================================

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS feat_1m;

CREATE TABLE feat_1m (
    instId      TEXT NOT NULL,
    ts          INTEGER NOT NULL,                  -- timestamp en ms
    open        REAL DEFAULT 0,
    high        REAL DEFAULT 0,
    low         REAL DEFAULT 0,
    close       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    volume      REAL DEFAULT 0,
    price       REAL DEFAULT 0,

    ema12       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ema26       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ema20       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ema50       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ema100      REAL DEFAULT 0,
    ema200      REAL DEFAULT 0,

    rsi7        REAL DEFAULT 0,
    rsi14       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    macd        REAL DEFAULT 0,
    macd_signal REAL DEFAULT 0,
    macd_hist   REAL DEFAULT 0,

    atr         REAL DEFAULT 0,
    bb_up       REAL DEFAULT 0,
    bb_mid      REAL DEFAULT 0,
    bb_low      REAL DEFAULT 0,
    bb_width    REAL DEFAULT 0,

    adx         REAL DEFAULT 0,
    plus_di     REAL DEFAULT 0,
    minus_di    REAL DEFAULT 0,

    trigger     TEXT DEFAULT '',
    ctx         TEXT DEFAULT 'range',

    ts_update   INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now')*1000),
    PRIMARY KEY (instId, ts)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_feat1m_inst ON feat_1m(instId);
CREATE INDEX idx_feat1m_ts ON feat_1m(ts);

-- ============================================================
-- Vue de contrôle rapide
-- ============================================================
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_feat_1m_overview AS
SELECT
  instId,
  datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update,
  COUNT(*) AS n_rows,
  ROUND(AVG(close),6) AS avg_close
FROM feat_1m
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY instId;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/recorder_enhance_H.sql -----
-- ======================================================
-- RECORDER H PERFORMANCE ENHANCEMENT
-- ======================================================

-- Nettoyage préalable
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_coin;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_setup;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_coin_setup;

-- === SCORE H COIN (EMA par actif) ===
CREATE VIEW v_H_coin AS
WITH ranked AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        score_H,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts_record DESC) AS n
    FROM trades_record
)
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(SUM(score_H * POWER(0.9, n-1)) / SUM(POWER(0.9, n-1)), 4) AS score_H_coin,
    COUNT(*) AS trades_count,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN score_H > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)*100.0/COUNT(*),1) AS winrate
FROM ranked
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY score_H_coin DESC;

-- === SCORE H SETUP (EMA par setup/entry_reason) ===
CREATE VIEW v_H_setup AS
WITH ranked AS (
    SELECT
        entry_reason,
        score_H,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY entry_reason ORDER BY ts_record DESC) AS n
    FROM trades_record
)
SELECT
    entry_reason,
    ROUND(SUM(score_H * POWER(0.9, n-1)) / SUM(POWER(0.9, n-1)), 4) AS score_H_setup,
    COUNT(*) AS trades_count,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN score_H > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)*100.0/COUNT(*),1) AS winrate
FROM ranked
GROUP BY entry_reason
ORDER BY score_H_setup DESC;

-- === SCORE H COIN x SETUP (EMA croisé) ===
CREATE VIEW v_H_coin_setup AS
WITH ranked AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        entry_reason,
        score_H,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY instId, entry_reason ORDER BY ts_record DESC) AS n
    FROM trades_record
)
SELECT
    instId,
    entry_reason,
    ROUND(SUM(score_H * POWER(0.9, n-1)) / SUM(POWER(0.9, n-1)), 4) AS score_H_pair,
    COUNT(*) AS trades_count,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN score_H > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)*100.0/COUNT(*),1) AS winrate
FROM ranked
GROUP BY instId, entry_reason
ORDER BY score_H_pair DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/recorder_schema.sql -----
PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF;

DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS v_perf_summary;
DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS v_H_coin;
DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS v_H_setup;
DROP VIEW  IF EXISTS v_H_coin_setup;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS trades_record;

CREATE TABLE trades_record (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,
    pnl REAL,
    score_H REAL,
    reason_exit TEXT,
    entry_reason TEXT,
    ctx TEXT,
    ts_close INTEGER
);

CREATE VIEW v_perf_summary AS
SELECT
    COUNT(*) AS total,
    SUM(CASE WHEN pnl>0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wins,
    SUM(CASE WHEN pnl<=0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS losses,
    ROUND(AVG(pnl),6) AS avg_pnl,
    ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H
FROM trades_record;

CREATE VIEW v_H_coin AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H,
    COUNT(*) AS n,
    ROUND(SUM(pnl),6) AS sum_pnl
FROM trades_record
GROUP BY instId;

CREATE VIEW v_H_setup AS
SELECT
    entry_reason,
    ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H,
    COUNT(*) AS n,
    ROUND(SUM(pnl),6) AS sum_pnl
FROM trades_record
GROUP BY entry_reason;

CREATE VIEW v_H_coin_setup AS
SELECT
    instId,
    entry_reason,
    ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H,
    COUNT(*) AS n,
    ROUND(SUM(pnl),6) AS sum_pnl
FROM trades_record
GROUP BY instId, entry_reason;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/recorder_schema_full.sql -----
PRAGMA foreign_keys=OFF;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_perf_summary;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_coin;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_setup;
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_H_coin_setup;
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS trades_record;

CREATE TABLE trades_record (
    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,
    pnl_raw REAL,
    pnl_net REAL,
    score_U REAL,
    score_A REAL,
    score_B REAL,
    score_H REAL,
    reason_exit TEXT,
    entry_reason TEXT,
    ctx TEXT,
    be_active INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    trail_active INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    pyr_level INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    ts_open INTEGER,
    ts_close INTEGER,
    duration_s REAL,
    ts_record INTEGER DEFAULT (strftime('%s','now'))
);

CREATE VIEW v_perf_summary AS
SELECT
    COUNT(*) AS total,
    SUM(CASE WHEN pnl_net>0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS wins,
    SUM(CASE WHEN pnl_net<=0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS losses,
    ROUND(AVG(pnl_net),6) AS avg_pnl,
    ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H
FROM trades_record;

CREATE VIEW v_H_coin AS
SELECT instId,
       ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H,
       COUNT(*) AS n,
       ROUND(SUM(pnl_net),6) AS sum_pnl
FROM trades_record
GROUP BY instId;

CREATE VIEW v_H_setup AS
SELECT entry_reason,
       ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H,
       COUNT(*) AS n,
       ROUND(SUM(pnl_net),6) AS sum_pnl
FROM trades_record
GROUP BY entry_reason;

CREATE VIEW v_H_coin_setup AS
SELECT instId,
       entry_reason,
       ROUND(AVG(score_H),6) AS avg_H,
       COUNT(*) AS n,
       ROUND(SUM(pnl_net),6) AS sum_pnl
FROM trades_record
GROUP BY instId, entry_reason;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/signal_triggers.sql -----
PRAGMA journal_mode = WAL;
PRAGMA synchronous = NORMAL;

ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/gest.db' AS gest;

CREATE TRIGGER IF NOT EXISTS trg_signal_new
AFTER INSERT ON signals_B
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO gest.bus_events (src, instId, event)
    VALUES ('signal', NEW.instId, 'NEW_SIGNAL');
END;

DETACH DATABASE gest;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/signals.sql -----
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS signals;
CREATE TABLE signals (
    instId TEXT,
    side TEXT,
    ctx TEXT,
    score_U REAL,
    score_A REAL,
    score_B REAL,
    reason TEXT,
    ts_signal INTEGER
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_signals_inst_ts ON signals(instId, ts_signal DESC);
DROP VIEW IF EXISTS signals_for_open;
CREATE VIEW signals_for_open AS
SELECT instId, side, ctx, score_U, score_A, score_B, reason, ts_signal
FROM signals
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/signals_schema.sql -----
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS signals;
CREATE TABLE signals(
    instId     TEXT,
    ts_signal  INTEGER,
    side       TEXT,
    ctx        TEXT,
    score_U    REAL,
    score_A    REAL,
    score_B    REAL,
    reason     TEXT
);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sig_inst ON signals(instId);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sig_ts   ON signals(ts_signal DESC);

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS signals_for_open;
CREATE VIEW signals_for_open AS
SELECT *
FROM signals
ORDER BY ts_signal DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/v_signals_for_open.sql -----
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_signals_for_open AS
SELECT
  f.instId,
  f.side,
  f.reason,
  f.price,
  f.atr,
  f.score_B,
  f.ts_signal
FROM signals_B AS f
WHERE f.price > 0
ORDER BY f.ts_signal DESC;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/v_signals_last10.sql -----
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_signals_last10 AS
SELECT
    instId,
    side,
    reason,
    ctx,
    ROUND(price,6) AS price,
    ROUND(score_B,2) AS score_B,
    strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S', ts, 'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
    printf('%02d:%02d', (strftime('%s','now') - ts)/60, (strftime('%s','now') - ts)%60) AS age_hms
FROM signals_B
ORDER BY ts DESC
LIMIT 10;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/view_feat_1m.sql -----
ATTACH DATABASE '/opt/scalp/project/data/ob.db' AS ob;

DROP VIEW IF EXISTS v_feat_1m;

CREATE VIEW v_feat_1m AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ts,
    o,
    h,
    l,
    c,
    v,
    AVG(c) OVER w12 AS ema12,
    (c - LAG(c) OVER w) AS mom,
    ((c / LAG(c) OVER w) - 1) * 100 AS roc,
    CASE
        WHEN LAG(AVG(c) OVER w12) OVER w IS NULL THEN NULL
        ELSE (AVG(c) OVER w12 - LAG(AVG(c) OVER w12) OVER w)
    END AS slope
FROM ob.ohlcv_1m
WINDOW
    w AS (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts),
    w12 AS (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts ROWS 12 PRECEDING);

DETACH DATABASE ob;

----- FILE: /opt/scalp/project/sql/x_schema.sql -----
-- =====================================================
-- X.DB  (Open, Follow, History, Views, Indexes)
-- =====================================================

-- POSITIONS OUVERTES
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS positions_open (
    instId      TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    side        TEXT,
    entry       REAL,
    sl          REAL,
    tp          REAL,
    qty         REAL,
    score_U     REAL,
    score_A     REAL,
    score_B     REAL,
    ts_open     INTEGER
);

-- POSITIONS SUIVIES (SL/TP/BE/TRAIL)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS follow (
    instId      TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    side        TEXT,
    entry       REAL,
    sl          REAL,
    tp          REAL,
    be_active   INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    trail_active INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    atr         REAL,
    ts_update   INTEGER
);

-- HISTORIQUE
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS x_history (
    id          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
    instId      TEXT,
    side        TEXT,
    entry       REAL,
    exit        REAL,
    pnl         REAL,
    score_U     REAL,
    score_A     REAL,
    score_B     REAL,
    ts_open     INTEGER,
    ts_close    INTEGER
);

-- ===== VUES =====

-- Dernière ATR 1m
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_atr1m AS
SELECT instId, atr, ts
FROM ob_atr_1m
WHERE ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ob_atr_1m AS t2 WHERE t2.instId = ob_atr_1m.instId);

-- Dernier signal B pour X
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS signals_for_open AS
SELECT instId, side, ctx, score_U, score_A, score_B, ts_signal
FROM signals
WHERE ts_signal = (SELECT MAX(ts_signal) FROM signals s2 WHERE s2.instId = signals.instId);

-- Suivi des positions (open + ATR)
CREATE VIEW IF NOT EXISTS v_positions_follow AS
SELECT p.instId, p.side, p.entry, f.sl, f.tp, f.atr, f.be_active, f.trail_active
FROM positions_open p
LEFT JOIN follow f ON p.instId = f.instId;

-- ===== INDEXES =====
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_positions_open_inst ON positions_open(instId);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_follow_inst ON follow(instId);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_x_history_inst ON x_history(instId);

-- VIEWS --
v_ctx_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ctx_latest AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ctx,
    score_A
FROM ctx_A_latest
v_ohlcv_freshness|CREATE VIEW v_ohlcv_freshness AS
SELECT instId, '5m' AS tf,
       COUNT(*) AS n_candles,
       MAX(ts) AS ts_last,
       datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_local,
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM ohlcv_5m
GROUP BY instId
UNION ALL
SELECT instId, '15m',
       COUNT(*), MAX(ts),
       datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime'),
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1)
FROM ohlcv_15m
GROUP BY instId
UNION ALL
SELECT instId, '30m',
       COUNT(*), MAX(ts),
       datetime(MAX(ts)/1000,'unixepoch','localtime'),
       ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - MAX(ts))/1000.0,1)
FROM ohlcv_30m
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY tf, age_s ASC

-- VIEWS --
v_feat_1m|CREATE VIEW v_feat_1m AS
SELECT *,
       (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts) AS age_ms
FROM feat_1m
v_feat_3m|CREATE VIEW v_feat_3m AS
SELECT *,
       (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts) AS age_ms
FROM feat_3m
v_feat_5m|CREATE VIEW v_feat_5m AS
SELECT *,
       (strftime('%s','now')*1000 - ts) AS age_ms
FROM feat_5m
v_opener_for_gest|CREATE VIEW v_opener_for_gest AS
SELECT
  b.instId,
  b.side,
  b.price,
  b.atr,
  b.score_B,
  COALESCE(c.score_A,0) AS score_A,
  COALESCE(c.score_U,0) AS score_U,
  COALESCE(c.ctx,'range') AS ctx,
  b.reason,
  b.ts_signal
FROM signals_B b
LEFT JOIN ctx_cache c
  ON c.instId = b.instId
WHERE b.price>0
ORDER BY b.ts_signal DESC
v_signals_for_open|CREATE VIEW v_signals_for_open AS
SELECT
  f.instId,
  f.side,
  f.reason,
  f.price,
  f.atr,
  f.score_B,
  f.ts_signal
FROM signals_B AS f
WHERE f.price > 0
ORDER BY f.ts_signal DESC
v_signals_overview|CREATE VIEW v_signals_overview AS
SELECT
    s.instId,
    s.side,
    s.reason,
    s.score_B,
    s.ctx,
    datetime(s.ts_signal/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
    ROUND((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - s.ts_signal)/1000.0,1) AS age_s
FROM signals_B s
WHERE s.ts_signal = (
    SELECT MAX(ts_signal)
    FROM signals_B s2
    WHERE s2.instId = s.instId
)

-- INDEXES --
idx_bus_out_ack|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack)
idx_bus_out_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ts ON bus_out(ts)

[TABLE: budget_state]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|balance|REAL|0|1000.0|0
2|margin|REAL|0|0.0|0
3|pnl_real|REAL|0|0.0|0
4|ts_update|INTEGER|0||0

[TABLE: ledger]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|src|TEXT|0||0
2|instId|TEXT|0||0
3|side|TEXT|0||0
4|type|TEXT|0||0
5|amount|REAL|0||0
6|ts|INTEGER|0|strftime('%s','now')*1000|0

[TABLE: v_budget_overview]
0|balance||0||0
1|margin||0||0
2|pnl_real||0||0
3|last_update||0||0

[TABLE: bus_out]
0|id|INTEGER|0||1
1|instId|TEXT|0||0
2|event|TEXT|0||0
3|ts|INTEGER|0|strftime('%s','now')*1000|0
4|ack|INTEGER|0|0|0
5|payload|TEXT|0||0
6|src|TEXT|0||0

[TABLE: v_balance]
0|balance_usdt||0||0

[TABLE: v_exposure]
0|instId|TEXT|0||0
1|margin||0||0
2|pnl_real||0||0

-- VIEWS --
v_balance|CREATE VIEW v_balance AS
SELECT ROUND(SUM(CASE
  WHEN type IN ('deposit','pnl_real') THEN amount
  WHEN type='withdraw' THEN -amount
  ELSE 0 END),6) AS balance_usdt
FROM ledger
v_budget_overview|CREATE VIEW v_budget_overview AS
SELECT
  ROUND(balance,6) AS balance,
  ROUND(margin,6)  AS margin,
  ROUND(pnl_real,6) AS pnl_real,
  datetime(ts_update,'unixepoch','localtime') AS last_update
FROM budget_state
v_exposure|CREATE VIEW v_exposure AS
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='margin' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS margin,
    ROUND(SUM(CASE WHEN type='pnl_real' THEN amount ELSE 0 END),6) AS pnl_real
FROM ledger
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY ABS(margin) DESC

-- INDEXES --
idx_bus_out_ack|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack)
idx_bus_out_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ts ON bus_out(ts)

-- VIEWS --
v_activity_last_5min|CREATE VIEW v_activity_last_5min AS
SELECT stage, dest,
       COUNT(*) AS recent_msgs
FROM bus
WHERE ts > (strftime('%s','now')-300)*1000
GROUP BY stage, dest
v_last_msg|CREATE VIEW v_last_msg AS
SELECT stage, dest, instId,
       datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local,
       payload
FROM bus
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 50
v_pending|CREATE VIEW v_pending AS
SELECT stage, dest, COUNT(*) AS pending
FROM bus
WHERE ack=0
GROUP BY stage, dest
v_pipeline_health|CREATE VIEW v_pipeline_health AS
SELECT dest,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ack=0) AS pending,
       COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE ack=1) AS processed,
       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_activity
FROM bus
GROUP BY dest

-- INDEXES --

idx_bus_stage|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_stage ON bus(stage)
idx_bus_stage_dest_ack|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_stage_dest_ack ON bus(stage, dest, ack, ts)
idx_bus_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_ts ON bus(ts)

-- VIEWS --
v_active_positions|CREATE VIEW v_active_positions AS
SELECT trade_uid, instId, side, ts_open
FROM trades
WHERE state IN ('OPENING','ACTIVE')
v_bus_count|CREATE VIEW v_bus_count AS
SELECT src, event, COUNT(*) AS total, 
       MAX(datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')) AS last_ts
FROM bus_events
GROUP BY src, event
ORDER BY last_ts DESC
v_bus_latest|CREATE VIEW v_bus_latest AS
SELECT src, instId, event, datetime(ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
FROM bus_events
ORDER BY id DESC
LIMIT 50
v_for_closer|CREATE VIEW v_for_closer   AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state='CLOSING'
v_for_follower|CREATE VIEW v_for_follower AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state IN ('OPENING','ACTIVE')
v_for_opener|CREATE VIEW v_for_opener   AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state='NEW'
v_for_recorder|CREATE VIEW v_for_recorder AS SELECT * FROM trades_all WHERE state='CLOSED'
v_trades_overview|CREATE VIEW v_trades_overview AS
SELECT instId, side, status,
       datetime(ts_open/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_open_local,
       CASE WHEN ts_close>0 THEN datetime(ts_close/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') END AS ts_close_local,
       round(pnl,4) AS pnl
FROM trades_all
ORDER BY ts_open DESC
v_trades_with_open|CREATE VIEW v_trades_with_open AS
SELECT t.trade_uid, t.instId, t.side, t.state, t.ts_open
FROM trades t
WHERE t.ts_open IS NOT NULL

idx_bus_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_ts ON bus_events(ts)
idx_events_uid_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_events_uid_ts ON events(trade_uid, ts)

idx_trades_state|CREATE INDEX idx_trades_state    ON trades(state)

SELECT instId, ts, open, high, low, close, volume
FROM ohlcv_15m
WHERE ts IN (
  SELECT ts FROM ohlcv_15m AS o2
  WHERE o2.instId = ohlcv_15m.instId
  ORDER BY ts DESC
  LIMIT 150
)

FROM ohlcv_30m

  LIMIT 150
)

-- VIEWS --
v_atr_1m_latest|CREATE VIEW v_atr_1m_latest AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        ts,
        o,
        h,
        l,
        c,
        LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts) AS prev_close
    FROM ohlcv_1m
),
tr_calc AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        ts,
        MAX(
            h - l,
            ABS(h - prev_close),
            ABS(l - prev_close)
        ) AS tr
    FROM base
)
SELECT
    instId,
    ROUND(AVG(tr), 6) AS atr,
    MAX(ts) AS ts
FROM tr_calc
GROUP BY instId
ORDER BY instId
v_feat_1m_latest|CREATE VIEW v_feat_1m_latest AS
WITH base AS (
    SELECT
        instId,
        ts,
        o, h, l, c,
        LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts) AS prev_c
    FROM ohlcv_1m
),
tr AS (
    SELECT
        instId, ts,
        MAX(
            h - l,
            ABS(h - prev_c),
            ABS(l - prev_c)
        ) AS tr
    FROM base
),
atr_calc AS (
    SELECT
        instId, ts,
        AVG(tr) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING) AS atr14
    FROM tr
),
ema_calc AS (
    SELECT
        instId, ts, c,
        AVG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts ROWS 8 PRECEDING) AS ema_fast,
        AVG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts ROWS 20 PRECEDING) AS ema_slow
    FROM ohlcv_1m
),
rsi_base AS (
    SELECT
        instId, ts, c,
        MAX(c - LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts), 0) AS gain,
        MAX(LAG(c) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts) - c, 0) AS loss
    FROM ohlcv_1m
),
rsi_calc AS (
    SELECT
        instId, ts,
        100 - (100 / (1 + NULLIF(AVG(gain) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING)
                           / NULLIF(AVG(loss) OVER (PARTITION BY instId ORDER BY ts ROWS 13 PRECEDING),0),0))) AS rsi14
    FROM rsi_base
)
SELECT
    f.instId,
    f.ts,
    ROUND(r.rsi14, 2) AS rsi,
    ROUND(e.ema_fast, 6) AS ema_fast,
    ROUND(e.ema_slow, 6) AS ema_slow,
    ROUND(a.atr14, 6) AS atr
FROM ema_calc e
JOIN rsi_calc r ON r.instId=e.instId AND r.ts=e.ts
JOIN atr_calc a ON a.instId=e.instId AND a.ts=e.ts
JOIN ohlcv_1m f ON f.instId=e.instId AND f.ts=e.ts
WHERE e.ts >= (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM ohlcv_1m) - 300
ORDER BY f.instId, f.ts DESC
v_feat_latest|CREATE VIEW v_feat_latest AS
SELECT '1m' AS tf,
       f1.instId,
       f1.close,
       f1.ts,
       datetime(f1.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local
  FROM feat_1m f1
 WHERE f1.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_1m f2 WHERE f2.instId=f1.instId)
UNION ALL
SELECT '3m', f3.instId, f3.close, f3.ts,
       datetime(f3.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
  FROM feat_3m f3
 WHERE f3.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_3m f4 WHERE f4.instId=f3.instId)
UNION ALL
SELECT '5m', f5.instId, f5.close, f5.ts,
       datetime(f5.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime')
  FROM feat_5m f5
 WHERE f5.ts = (SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_5m f6 WHERE f6.instId=f5.instId)
v_feat_overview|CREATE VIEW v_feat_overview AS
SELECT f1.instId,
       f1.close AS close_1m,
       f3.close AS close_3m,
       f5.close AS close_5m,
       f1.ema12 AS ema12_1m,
       f3.ema12 AS ema12_3m,
       f5.ema12 AS ema12_5m,
       f1.ema26 AS ema26_1m,
       f3.ema26 AS ema26_3m,
       f5.ema26 AS ema26_5m,
       f1.rsi14 AS rsi14_1m,
       f3.rsi14 AS rsi14_3m,
       f5.rsi14 AS rsi14_5m,
       f1.ts AS ts_1m,
       f3.ts AS ts_3m,
       f5.ts AS ts_5m,
       datetime(f1.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local_1m,
       datetime(f3.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local_3m,
       datetime(f5.ts/1000,'unixepoch','localtime') AS ts_local_5m
  FROM feat_1m f1
  LEFT JOIN feat_3m f3 ON f3.instId=f1.instId
  LEFT JOIN feat_5m f5 ON f5.instId=f1.instId
 WHERE f1.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_1m f WHERE f.instId=f1.instId)
   AND f3.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_3m f WHERE f.instId=f3.instId)
   AND f5.ts=(SELECT MAX(ts) FROM feat_5m f WHERE f.instId=f5.instId)

-- INDEXES --

idx_5m_inst_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_5m_inst_ts ON ohlcv_5m(instId, ts)
idx_bus_out_ack|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ack ON bus_out(ack)
idx_bus_out_ts|CREATE INDEX idx_bus_out_ts  ON bus_out(ts)

sqlite_autoindex_ohlcv_5m_1|

-- VIEWS --
v_ticks_latest|CREATE VIEW v_ticks_latest AS
SELECT
  t.instId,
  t.lastPr,
  t.ts,
  strftime('%H:%M:%S', t.ts/1000, 'unixepoch','localtime') AS hms,
  printf('%02d:%02d:%02d',
     ((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - t.ts)/1000)/3600,
     (((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - t.ts)/1000)%3600)/60,
     ((strftime('%s','now')*1000 - t.ts)/1000)%60) AS age_hms
FROM ticks t
ORDER BY t.instId
